# Engine log

The dated narrative for material engine changes — the third layer of the four-layer trace system named in [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md) (ADRs / engine log / MemPalace `decision`-tagged drawers / git history). The "engine" is the AI build apparatus the user and Claude run together to construct Paideia: session lifecycle, validators, hooks, MemPalace integration, operations docs, ADRs about how the AI works. This file is **not** Paideia's product release log; that role is reserved for [`CHANGELOG.md`](CHANGELOG.md), which carries a reserved-stub preamble until Phase 9 release prep authors the v1.0.0 entry. Per [ADR 0037](adr/0037-engine-product-wall-and-changelog-rename.md), the reservation is explicit at the filename layer so a future contributor or session walking up cold does not re-create the file under conventional Keep-a-Changelog assumptions.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/) with project-specific calibration: changes are scoped to **state-of-record** engine artifacts (design docs, schemas, seed graph migrations, build_plan, ADRs, OPERATIONS-equivalent docs, top-level project files). Application code (React, API endpoints, UI) is **git-only** — its history lives in the commit log, not here.

This project does not yet follow [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/) — versions are milestones (`0.0.x` for foundation; `0.1.0` at foundation close; later versions track product readiness).

---

## [Unreleased]

### Added (S-0075 — Phase 5 cross-bridges seed; P5-11 complete; P5-12 closeout now eligible for the first time — final remaining Phase 5 task; seventh load-bearing routine-mode exercise of apply_migration.py wrapper)
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0060_seed_crossbridges_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0060_seed_crossbridges_part1.sql) — first Phase 5 cross-bridges file (P5-11 range 0060-0069); 71 cross-domain `pedagogical_prerequisite` edges across the 380-node Phase 5 graph; **zero new nodes** (every endpoint references a pre-existing seeded id from one of the 14 prior subdomain migrations). Three groupings per [phase_5.md](build_readiness/phase_5.md) T2-G #1: **(A) Service-node → philosophy-subdomain bridges (45 edges)** subdivided into (A1) 15 service formal-logic → philosophy edges (truth_value / bivalence_principle / argument_logical / validity_logical / soundness_logical / inference_rule / modus_ponens / modus_tollens / formal_proof / counterexample → classical_logic / propositional_logic / predicate_logic / dialetheism / fuzzy_logic / paraconsistent_logic / formal_epistemology / epistemic_justification / falsificationism / gettier_problem); (A2) 12 service math → philosophy edges (set_mathematical / quantifier / probability_mathematical / conditional_probability / bayes_theorem / expected_value → russell_paradox / possible_worlds / kripke_semantics / predicate_logic / bayesian_epistemology / bayesianism_confirmation / conditionalization / dutch_book_argument / utilitarianism / social_contract_theory); (A3) 18 service history terminators → philosophy edges (aristotelian_four_causes / greek_atomism / scholasticism / renaissance_mechanism / vienna_circle_logical_positivism → causation / essence_metaphysical / scientific_explanation / humean_regularity_theory / physicalism / reductionism_in_science / mereological_nihilism / realism_about_universals / divine_command_theory / substance_dualism / scientific_theory / scientific_method / verificationism / falsificationism / demarcation_problem / tarskis_t_schema / deductive_nomological_model / behaviorism_logical). **(B) Within-philosophy cross-subdomain bridges (26 edges)** organized by source-subdomain: epistemology↔mind/language/science/logic; metaphysics↔mind/logic; mind↔language/science; logic↔science; ethics↔mind/political. **(C) Aesthetics deferred** to a future part2 if telemetry warrants (sub-range slots 0061-0069 reserved). Each edge carries an in-line comment in 0060 explaining the pedagogical-prerequisite warrant; the candidate set across the 14 prior seedings collectively named ~150 cross-bridges, pruned to the 71 with highest pedagogical warrant and tightest concept-level connection. graph_version 15→16. Applied to `paideia-dev` via [`engine/tools/apply_migration.py`](tools/apply_migration.py) wrapper; recorded in `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations` as version `20260505232807`. **Seventh load-bearing routine-mode exercise of the apply_migration.py wrapper** (first S-0066 P5-07a; second S-0068 P5-06; third S-0070 P5-07b; fourth S-0071 P5-08; fifth S-0073 P5-09 — including the durably-confirmed first-routine-exercise of the wrapper's exit-3 SQL-error rollback path; sixth S-0074 P5-10) — first apply attempt succeeded cleanly. The cross-bridges migration is qualitatively distinct from the six prior subdomain seeds in being edges-only rather than nodes+edges; the wrapper handles the shape transparently. Pre-apply Python audit confirmed: 0 dangling endpoints (all 142 endpoints reference seeded ids), 0 UNIQUE collisions (consistent with phase_5.md T2-G #1's containment guarantee — no prior subdomain seed authored cross-domain edges), 0 self-loops, 0 cycles in the combined 536-edge graph (existing 465 + new 71). The wrapper's first-apply-success path is now durably confirmed across seven routine fires.

### Changed (S-0075 — Phase 5 cross-bridges seed; P5-11 complete)
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md) — removed `cross_domain_dependency` reserved-but-unused row per the [phase_5.md](build_readiness/phase_5.md) T1-E / T3-B decision adjudicated in-session at S-0075. Decision: **do NOT promote `cross_domain_dependency`** to the v1 registry; continue the existing disjoint-domain convention. Reasoning: every cross-domain edge authored in 0060 is shape-identical to within-domain `pedagogical_prerequisite` (same predicate semantics, same domain/range typing, same downstream consumer behavior); the only distinguishing feature is the disjoint-domain shape that validate.py's `suspicious_cross_domain_ratio` already detects per [phase_4_graph_validation.md](build_readiness/phase_4_graph_validation.md) T2-D and [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) lines 1276-1278; registering would require downstream consumer changes (traversal, syllabus generation, mastery computation per phase_4_graph_validation.md T2-G consume `pedagogical_prerequisite` only) outside this routine session's scope; the manifest itself recommended "promote if Phase 5 cross-domain authoring surfaces a structural distinction" — and the authoring did NOT surface one. Per the manifest's own discipline ("If a reserved entry never gets used by the time the next periodic project health check fires, it should be removed from this list"), the row is removed in the same commit as the cross-bridges migration that empirically grounds the decision. A note in the section preface records the S-0075 decision and forward-cites 0060.

Four cross-cluster service-to-service bridges (axiom_mathematical → formal_proof tying math to formal-logic; aristotelian_four_causes / renaissance_mechanism / hegelian_dialectic → vienna_circle_logical_positivism tying the historical chain to the founding of analytic philosophy). 25/25 INTERPRETED; within-service edges only (cross-domain bridges from service nodes to philosophy-subdomain nodes — bayes_theorem ↔ bayesian_epistemology / bayesianism_confirmation; modus_ponens / quantifier / set_mathematical ↔ propositional_logic / predicate_logic / russell_paradox; aristotelian_four_causes ↔ causation; greek_atomism ↔ physicalism / reductionism; renaissance_mechanism ↔ substance_dualism; vienna_circle_logical_positivism ↔ verificationism / falsificationism / demarcation_problem; hegelian_dialectic ↔ critique-of-metaphysics positions across multiple subdomains — all deferred to P5-11). graph_version 14→15. ### Added (S-0073 — Phase 5 philosophy-of-science methodology-anchored core seed; P5-09 complete; fifth load-bearing routine-mode exercise of apply_migration.py wrapper including durable confirmation of the SQL-error rollback path)
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0080_seed_science_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0080_seed_science_part1.sql) — first Phase 5 philosophy-of-science file (P5-09 range 0080-0089); 27 nodes + 30 edges across the nine methodology-anchored clusters per [phase_5.md](build_readiness/phase_5.md) T1-B (foundation: philosophy_of_science/scientific_method/scientific_theory; confirmation: hypothetico_deductivism/bayesianism_confirmation/paradox_of_the_ravens — Hume's problem of induction is canonical-homed under epistemology in P5-01a so the within-confirmation-cluster edges scientific_method→problem_of_induction and problem_of_induction→bayesianism_confirmation are cross-domain and deferred to P5-11; demarcation and structure: demarcation_problem/falsificationism (Popper 1934/59)/paradigm (Kuhn 1962 SSR)/paradigm_shift/research_programme (Lakatos 1970); theories of explanation: scientific_explanation/deductive_nomological_model (Hempel-Oppenheim 1948)/inference_to_the_best_explanation (Lipton/Harman)/unification_theory_of_explanation (Friedman/Kitcher); realism and antirealism: scientific_realism/constructive_empiricism (van Fraassen 1980)/no_miracles_argument (Putnam/Boyd)/pessimistic_meta_induction (Laudan 1981); underdetermination and observation: underdetermination/duhem_quine_thesis/theory_ladenness_of_observation (Hanson/Kuhn/Feyerabend); laws and models: law_of_nature/scientific_model; reduction and unity: reductionism_in_science/multiple_realizability_in_science (Putnam 1967 → Fodor 1974); values in science: value_free_ideal). 6-tier layered DAG rooted at philosophy_of_science with three cross-cluster bridges (falsificationism→paradigm reflecting the Popper-Kuhn debate; duhem_quine_thesis→paradigm reflecting Quinean confirmational holism converging with historicist paradigm-relativism; duhem_quine_thesis→theory_ladenness_of_observation reflecting the holist→Hanson-Kuhn-Feyerabend chain) plus the load-bearing T1→T4 skip-tier scientific_theory→paradigm. 27/27 INTERPRETED; within-domain edges only (cross-domain bridges to epistemology on Hume/induction/holism, metaphysics on natural kinds and laws, philosophy of mind on multiple realizability and functionalism, ethics on values in inquiry, philosophy of language on verificationism — all deferred to P5-11). graph_version 13→14. Applied to `paideia-dev` via [`engine/tools/apply_migration.py`](tools/apply_migration.py) wrapper; recorded in supabase_migrations.schema_migrations as version `20260505222912`. **Fifth load-bearing routine-mode exercise of the apply_migration.py wrapper** (first S-0066 P5-07a; second S-0068 P5-06; third S-0070 P5-07b; fourth S-0071 P5-08) — and notably the **first routine-mode exercise of the wrapper's exit-3 SQL-error path**: the first apply attempt failed with `nodes_pkey` UNIQUE-violation on `problem_of_induction` (already in DB as epistemology); the wrapper handled the failure cleanly (exit 3, body rolled back atomically by the migration's BEGIN/COMMIT wrap, no `schema_migrations` row inserted, post-failure snapshot confirmed zero `gv=14` nodes and unchanged `settings.graph_version=13`); after the canonical-home fix (drop conflicting node + two cross-domain edges), the second apply succeeded cleanly. The wrapper's behavior under SQL error in routine context is now durably confirmed.

### Added (S-0072 — routine close-out apparatus: parent main FF post-push and post-close worktree sweep)
- [`engine/tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py) — added `parent_ff()` helper and post-push invocation in `main()` for all three modes (eager-claim, deliverable, close). Closes the asymmetry vs interactive close where parent's local main was being left stale because the routine wrapper pushes from inside a linked worktree on a feature branch (`HEAD:main`). Best-effort: parent FF failure (parent on a non-target branch, uncommitted-change conflicts) is logged but does NOT propagate to the wrapper exit code; boot-freshness remains the safety net per [ADR 0052](adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md). After this change, parent main acquires `merge claude/<branch>: Fast-forward` entries (matching the interactive shape) instead of `merge refs/remotes/origin/main: Fast-forward` (the next session's reactive boot-freshness recovery). Symptom diagnosed in this conversation's own boot-freshness FF surface: every routine fire was needing the FF to catch up.
- [`engine/tools/routine_worktree_sweep.py`](tools/routine_worktree_sweep.py) — new tool, called from inside the worktree as the last action of routine close (after the close push and lock release). Removes the current session's worktree and its `claude/<name>` branch with the same pre-flight checks as `sweep_worktrees.sh` (claude/* branch, working tree clean, branch merged into main); refusals exit 2 with explicit reasons, generic git errors exit 5, both logged-and-continue (close has already succeeded — sweep is best-effort). The tool chdirs to parent BEFORE calling `git worktree remove` so child-process forks from this Python process don't fail on macOS once the worktree's CWD is unlinked. Closes the auto-clean follow-on named in [Issue #16](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/16).
- [`engine/tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py) — 7 new pytests for parent FF (32 total). Coverage: parent-path resolution from worktree vs parent, parent_ff success advances main, no-op when called from parent, refusal when parent on non-main branch, end-to-end main() with parent_ff success and failure paths.
- [`engine/tools/test_routine_worktree_sweep.py`](tools/test_routine_worktree_sweep.py) — new test file, 18 pytests. Covers helper unit behavior, all preflight refusal paths (parent invocation, dirty tree, non-claude/* branch, unmerged branch, detached HEAD), main() success / dry-run / refusal / cwd-default, and the chdir-before-sweep contract.

Closes [Issue #25](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/25).
- [`engine/session/archive/S-0057.json`](session/archive/S-0057.json), [`engine/session/archive/S-0067.json`](session/archive/S-0067.json) — close-out content recovered from stranded worktree state. Both archives were stuck on origin/main in a partial-close shape (status: in_progress, no outcome_summary, no scope_delivery, no outcome_summary_soft_warns); the actual close-out write-back was authored at session-end inside their respective worktrees (amazing-mayer-f501e9 / heuristic-gates-d71b84) but the close push did not propagate the archive writes. This is exactly the close-out gap pattern the new wrapper-side parent FF closes structurally going forward; the recovery clears the two known instances directly. [Issue #20](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/20)'s archive-history audit pass remains a separate follow-on.

### Changed (S-0069 — STATE.md size maintenance; rolling-window trim policy)
- [`engine/STATE.md`](STATE.md) — **one-time trim from ~35,456 tokens to ~6,000 tokens (25,155 bytes / 106 lines).** Four targeted edits: (1) 'Current phase' cell collapsed from 3,500-word session-history blob to a current-state summary sentence + ENGINE_LOG.md pointer; (2) all 13 'Prior build session' and 'Prior-prior build session' rows removed (S-0043 → S-0067; exact duplicates of ENGINE_LOG.md entries — the rolling-window design had no drop policy, so rows accumulated without bound); (3) stale historical paragraph from 'Next session work item' section pruned (referenced P5-06 as blocked, S-0059 context, and apply-mechanics findings all superseded by S-0064/S-0066/S-0068); (4) 'After S-0045' mini-changelog subsection removed (all entries fully captured in ENGINE_LOG.md). Nothing is lost: trimmed content is preserved in ENGINE_LOG.md narratives and `engine/session/archive/S-*.json` machine-readable records. Root cause: two accumulation patterns with no drop bound; MCP tool read limit (~25,000 tokens) exceeded at S-0069 boot. Deliverable commit `b28d9ea`.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — **rolling-window trim policy added** to the "Update STATE.md" step (step 4). Policy: after each session close, drop every row labeled 'Prior build session' or 'Prior-prior build session' — keep only the new 'Last build session' row plus one 'Prior build session' row at most. If STATE.md still exceeds ~20,000 tokens after the row drop, also collapse the 'Current phase' cell to the current-state summary form. Prevents the accumulation pattern that caused the S-0069 overflow from recurring.

### Added (S-0064 — apply-migration wrapper unblocks Phase 5 routine-mode after Production Reads gate regression)
- [`engine/adr/0055-apply-migration-wrapping-against-production-reads-gate.md`](adr/0055-apply-migration-wrapping-against-production-reads-gate.md) — **new ADR.** Names the auto-mode classifier's "Production Reads" gate as the failure mode (denies MCP supabase tools + ad-hoc psycopg from routine context with "Production Reads requires explicit user approval"; the gate is undocumented but real per a built-in `soft_deny` default; not configurable via per-MCP-tool allow rules). Introduces `engine/tools/apply_migration.py` as a parallel layer to ADR 0054's `routine_lifecycle_push.py`: harness gates Bash command surface, not subprocess-spawned operations from inside a permitted python tool. Trigger criterion #4 satisfied (8 surfaces).
- [`engine/tools/apply_migration.py`](tools/apply_migration.py) — the wrapper itself, ~360 lines. Three modes (default apply / `--dry-run` / `--force`). Mechanically shape-verifies HEAD before applying. Failure-mode discrimination via exit codes 0/2/3/4/5/6/7. Closes [Issue #18](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/18).
- [`engine/tools/test_apply_migration.py`](tools/test_apply_migration.py) — 24 pytests against psycopg-stub fixtures; stub `__spec__` set via `importlib.machinery.ModuleSpec` to bypass transitive `find_spec` from `_venv_reexec.ensure_venv_python`; module-level `_StubError` classes for shared exception identity.
- [`engine/build_readiness/apply_migration_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/apply_migration_first_exercise.md) — mechanism-first-exercise gate report per ADR 0053. T1-B/C/D/E resolved at S-0064; T1-A pending first routine fire post-S-0064.

- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0100_seed_political_philosophy_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0100_seed_political_philosophy_part1.sql) — **eighth Phase 5 seed migration; first political-philosophy file; closes the political-philosophy subdomain.** 28 nodes + 34 edges across four clusters per [phase_5.md](build_readiness/phase_5.md) T1-B "Political philosophy seed". **Foundation (1)**: political_philosophy. **Theories of justice (8)**: justice (Aristotelian distributive/corrective/procedural tripartite), distributive_justice (Rawls 1971 reframing; Nozick patterned-vs-historical contrast; Wilt Chamberlain argument), justice_as_fairness (Rawls 1971 — original position; veil of ignorance; two principles; difference principle; lexical-priority of liberty; Cohen 1995 critique), communitarianism (MacIntyre 1981 / Sandel 1982 / Walzer 1983 / Taylor 1989 — unencumbered-self critique; spheres-of-justice methodological critique; tradition-fragmentation argument), capability_approach (Sen 1980 / Nussbaum 2000 — substantive freedoms / functionings metric; UN HDI operationalization; central-capabilities list disagreement), luck_egalitarianism (Cohen 1989 / Arneson 1989 / Dworkin 1981 — choice/circumstance distinction; brute vs option luck; Anderson 1999 relational-egalitarian critique), desert_theory_political (Miller 1999 PRINCIPLES OF SOCIAL JUSTICE partial-revival against Rawls's morally-arbitrary critique). **State, authority, legitimacy (6)**: state_political (Weber 1919 territorial-monopoly definition; Westphalia 1648 institutionalization; cosmopolitan post-Westphalian challenges), sovereignty (Bodin 1576 SIX BOOKS OF THE COMMONWEALTH; Hobbes 1651; Westphalian state system; Krasner 1999 unbundling), political_authority (Raz 1986 service-conception / normal justification thesis / dependence + preemption theses; Wolff 1970 philosophical-anarchist challenge), political_legitimacy (consent / fair-play / democratic / instrumental theories; legitimacy-vs-justice-vs-authority distinctions), social_contract_theory (Hobbes 1651 LEVIATHAN / Locke 1689 SECOND TREATISE / Rousseau 1762 SOCIAL CONTRACT / Rawls 1971 hypothetical-consent restatement; Hume 1748 critique of tacit consent), political_obligation (Wolff 1970 / Simmons 1979 anarchist denial; consent / fair-play / gratitude / natural-duty / associative-obligations theories; Hart 1955 fair-play; Dworkin 1986 associative). **Liberty, equality, rights (7)**: liberty_political (Berlin 1958 TWO CONCEPTS — negative-vs-positive; Constant 1819 ancient-vs-modern; Pettit 1997 republican non-domination as third concept), equality_political (formal / opportunity / outcome / relational; Anderson 1999 relational-egalitarianism; Parfit 1995 leveling-down objection; Dworkin 2000 equal concern and respect), human_rights (UDHR 1948 / ICCPR 1966 / ICESCR 1966; Griffin 2008 ON HUMAN RIGHTS moral conception; Rawls 1999 LAW OF PEOPLES / Beitz 2009 THE IDEA OF HUMAN RIGHTS political conception), natural_rights (Locke 1689; Aquinas / Suarez / Grotius natural-law antecedents; Bentham 1843 nonsense-on-stilts critique; Marx 1843 possessive-individualism critique), positive_rights (welfare / education / healthcare; ICESCR 1966 codification; Marshall 1950 social-citizenship lineage), negative_rights (non-interference; Berlin / Nozick / classical-liberal default; ICCPR 1966 codification), toleration (Locke 1689 LETTER CONCERNING TOLERATION / Mill 1859 ON LIBERTY / Rawls 1993 POLITICAL LIBERALISM public reason; Popper 1945 paradox of tolerance; toleration-recognition distinction). **Government and political ideologies (6)**: democracy (intrinsic / instrumental / epistemic justifications; Estlund 2008 DEMOCRATIC AUTHORITY epistemic theory; Anderson 2006; Brennan 2016 AGAINST DEMOCRACY epistocratic challenge; deliberative-vs-aggregative), liberalism (Mill / Rawls comprehensive vs political; classical / egalitarian / political-liberal strands; communitarian / libertarian / Marxist / multicultural / feminist critiques), republicanism (Pettit 1997 REPUBLICANISM freedom-as-non-domination; Skinner 1998 LIBERTY BEFORE LIBERALISM historical recovery; Aristotelian-civic-humanist tradition vs neo-republican distinction), conservatism (Burke 1790 REFLECTIONS ON THE REVOLUTION IN FRANCE; Oakeshott 1962 RATIONALISM IN POLITICS; traditionalist / religious / fusionist strands; distinguished from libertarianism / fascism / reactionary politics), socialism (Marx 1867 CAPITAL labor theory of value + structural critique; Cohen 2009 WHY NOT SOCIALISM? camping-trip; revolutionary-vs-reformist; planned-vs-market socialism per Roemer 1994; democratic-socialism vs social-democracy distinction), multiculturalism (Kymlicka 1995 MULTICULTURAL CITIZENSHIP — national-minorities/immigrant-groups distinction; Taylor 1992 / Honneth 1995 recognition; Fraser 1995 redistribution-recognition debate; Okin 1999 IS MULTICULTURALISM BAD FOR WOMEN? minorities-within-minorities). All 28 nodes `confidence_level=INTERPRETED` (mirrors P5-01a/b/P5-02a/b/P5-03/P5-04a/b's 100%); all 34 edges `pedagogical_prerequisite`. `domain[]` exactly `{political}` for every node — cross-domain bridges (justice_as_fairness↔ethics contractualism; political_legitimacy/obligation↔ethics first-order normative theory; natural_rights↔ethics deontology; political_authority↔logic deontic; social_contract_theory↔mind collective-intentionality and language speech-acts; sovereignty↔metaphysics group ontology; democracy↔epistemology truth-tracking institutions; multiculturalism↔epistemology hermeneutical injustice + ethics recognition + language identity-terms; republicanism↔mind rational agency) deferred to P5-11. `provenance='ai-seed'` everywhere. `graph_version` 8 → 9 in same transaction as the 62 INSERTs. Edge structure: 5-tier layered DAG (T0 political_philosophy; T1 justice + state_political + liberty_political + equality_political + social_contract_theory; T2 distributive_justice + sovereignty + political_authority + negative_rights + positive_rights + natural_rights + liberalism + republicanism; T3 justice_as_fairness + libertarianism_political + communitarianism + capability_approach + desert_theory_political + democracy + political_legitimacy + political_obligation + human_rights + toleration + socialism; T4 luck_egalitarianism + conservatism + multiculturalism). Every edge points lower→higher tier so Kosaraju SCC check confirms acyclicity post-apply. Authored under task P5-05 of `T-PHASE-5` per [`engine/build_readiness/phase_5.md`](build_readiness/phase_5.md). **Apply mechanics (S-0058/S-0059 chunked-execute_sql + apply_migration-marker pattern continued)**: ~70KB executable SQL too large for single MCP `apply_migration`; applied via four `execute_sql` calls (UPDATE settings; INSERT 15 nodes — political_philosophy through republicanism; INSERT 13 nodes — justice_as_fairness through multiculturalism; INSERT 34 edges) in FK-safe order, then `apply_migration` with name `0100_seed_political_philosophy_part1` and no-op body recorded the migration name in `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations`. Pre-apply awk-grep escape sweep clean. ### Added (S-0060 — routine lifecycle-push wrapper; closes harness Default Branch Push gate)
- [`engine/adr/0054-lifecycle-push-wrapping-against-default-branch-push-gate.md`](adr/0054-lifecycle-push-wrapping-against-default-branch-push-gate.md) — **new ADR.** Names the local-routine "Default Branch Push" gate as the failure mode that blocked S-0059's eager-claim push from a routine session. Introduces `routine_lifecycle_push.py` as a fourth mechanical layer in [ADR 0052](adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md)'s freshness/lock/recovery family. The wrapper performs the push via `subprocess.run(["git", "push", ...])` from inside a permitted python tool — the harness gate inspects Bash command surface, not subprocess-spawned git operations. Each of three modes (`eager-claim`, `deliverable`, `close`) mechanically shape-verifies HEAD before pushing; refuses with explicit reject reason and exit 2 on any verification failure — actively safer than raw `git push` for lifecycle commits. Failure-mode discrimination via exit codes 0/2/3/4/5: 0 success, 2 verification refused (HANDOFF; no retry), 3 push rejected by remote (gate fired despite hypothesis OR non-fast-forward race), 4 network failure (retry once after 5s), 5 generic git error. Trigger-criterion evaluation per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) section: qualifies under #4 (Consequences span ≥ 5 tooling files) — first-exercise gate report is mandatory before unattended use.
- [`engine/tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py) — **the wrapper itself, ~410 lines.** Three modes per ADR 0054. Each verifier runs `git log`, `git rev-list --count`, `git status --porcelain`, `git diff --name-status` against `origin/main`, and (for eager-claim and close) reads register_state.json before and after via `git show`. The deliverable mode imports `check_routine_scope` for path-matching parity with the boot-time scope check. On verification refusal: prints `[routine-lifecycle-push] REFUSED ({mode}): <reason>` to stderr, names the local commit SHA, and exits 2 — does NOT amend, reset, or otherwise modify the repo (matches `routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`'s posture: bounded shape only; outside the shape, refuse).
- [`engine/tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py) — **21 pytests against tmp-dir bare-repo + clone fixtures.** Per the user's S-0060 directive ("test, test, test"). Coverage: 3 well-formed accepts (one per mode); 12 shape-verification rejects covering distinct predicates per mode (eager-claim: two-commits-ahead, subject-pattern-wrong, diff-touches-outside-set, register-state-doesnt-bump-one, current-json-already-existed; deliverable: chore(session)-prefix-reserved, subject-not-conventional-commits, path-outside-scope_lock, working-tree-dirty; close: archive-not-created, current-json-not-deleted, register-state-doesnt-flip, diff-touches-arbitrary); 3 push-failure paths (non-fast-forward returns 3, unreachable remote returns 4, missing remote returns 5); 3 edge cases (main refuses with exit 2 without pushing; --dry-run verifies but does not push). All green. Fixture pattern matches `test_routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`.
- [`engine/tools/probe_push_gate.py`](tools/probe_push_gate.py) — **Phase 0 empirical probe (~40 lines + 8 pytests).** Three modes: --dry-run (default, safe anywhere), --actually-push (empty commit + push to throwaway branch `claude/probe-push-gate-<UTC-timestamp>`), --actually-push --target-main (load-bearing test: pushes empty commit to main via subprocess). Phase 0 Run 2 result (S-0060): subprocess push to throwaway branch succeeded from interactive context (commit `dafaad6` on remote ref `claude/probe-push-gate-20260505T045706Z`); local HEAD soft-reset back to eager-claim. Phase 0 Run 3 (load-bearing — subprocess push to main from routine context) deferred to first routine fire post-S-0060 per the readiness note.
- [`engine/tools/test_probe_push_gate.py`](tools/test_probe_push_gate.py) — 8 pytests covering probe modes against tmp-dir bare-repo fixtures. All green.
- [`engine/build_readiness/routine_lifecycle_push_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/routine_lifecycle_push_first_exercise.md) — **mechanism-first-exercise gate report per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md).** Covers the wrapper's pre-flight: trigger-criterion evaluation (qualifies under #4), Phase 0 empirical findings (Run 1 baseline, Run 2 interactive subprocess success, Run 3 deferred-with-rationale), Tier 1 / Tier 2 / Tier 3 triage, cold-review prompts. T1-A (subprocess-bypass verification for routine context) closes at Phase 2 wrapper verification.

### Added (S-0059 — Phase 5 ethics applied seed; P5-04b complete; ethics subdomain fully seeded)
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0026_seed_ethics_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0026_seed_ethics_part1.sql) — **seventh Phase 5 seed migration; second ethics file; closes the ethics subdomain.** 28 nodes + 34 edges across three layers per [phase_5.md](build_readiness/phase_5.md) T1-B "Ethics applied (P5-04b) — bioethics, environmental ethics, applied moral problems". **Foundation (1)**: applied_ethics. **Bioethics (11)**: bioethics, medical_ethics (Hippocratic anchor; Beecher 1966 / Belmont 1979 framing), research_ethics (Nuremberg 1947 / Belmont 1979 / Common Rule 1991), end_of_life_ethics (Quinlan 1976 / Cruzan 1990 / Rachels 1975 / Foot 1967 / Brock 1992), reproductive_ethics (Thomson 1971 / Marquis 1989 / Warren 1973 / SisterSong reproductive justice / disability-rights expressivist objection), four_principles_bioethics (Beauchamp & Childress 1979 with common-morality grounding), autonomy_bioethical, beneficence, non_maleficence, justice_bioethical, informed_consent (Salgo 1957 / Canterbury 1972 / five-component framework). **Environmental ethics (11)**: environmental_ethics, anthropocentrism (strong + weak/Norton 1991 + Christian-stewardship), biocentrism (Schweitzer 1923 / Taylor 1986), ecocentrism (Leopold 1949 / Callicott / Regan environmental-fascism critique), deep_ecology (Naess 1973 eight-point platform / Earth First! / Bookchin critique), animal_ethics (Singer 1975 utilitarian + Regan 1983 deontological + Hursthouse 2006 virtue + Donovan & Adams 2007 care + Nussbaum 2006 capabilities + Donaldson & Kymlicka 2011 ZOOPOLIS), sentientism (Bentham 1789 / Singer 1975), climate_ethics (Gardiner 2011 perfect moral storm / Shue / Jamieson 2014), future_generations (longtermism + repugnant conclusion + asymmetry + temporal-discounting), intergenerational_justice (Rawls 1971 just savings / capabilities / sufficientarian / prioritarian), non_identity_problem (Parfit 1984 ch. 16 depletion-vs-conservation; person-affecting vs impersonal-outcome views). **Applied moral problems (5)**: just_war_theory (Augustine / Aquinas / Walzer 1977 / McMahan 2009; jus ad bellum / jus in bello / jus post bellum / jus ad vim), pacifism (absolute + contingent + religious + deontological + consequentialist + non-violent-resistance-pragmatism), business_ethics (Friedman 1970 shareholder vs Freeman 1984 stakeholder; CSR; ESG), technology_ethics (Heidegger / Mumford / Ellul / Wiener 1950 / Floridi; engineering ethics; algorithmic-bias and explainability frontiers), ai_ethics (Wallach & Allen 2009 / Russell 2019 / Bostrom 2014; near-term-fairness vs alignment vs existential-risk strands; OECD/EU/US governance regimes). All 28 nodes `confidence_level=INTERPRETED` (mirrors P5-01a/b/P5-02a/b/P5-03/P5-04a's 100%); all 34 edges `pedagogical_prerequisite`. `domain[]` exactly `{ethics}` for every node — cross-domain bridges (autonomy + consent into political philosophy + language; ai_ethics into mind + language + epistemology; non_identity into metaphysics; climate into philosophy of science; just_war into political philosophy; deep_ecology + ecocentrism into metaphysics; animal_ethics + sentientism into philosophy of mind) deferred to P5-11. Within-ethics cross-references back into P5-04a's metaethics+normative-theory inventory (autonomy_bioethical → kantian_ethics; informed_consent → deontology; future_generations → contractualism; intergenerational_justice → contractualism; business_ethics → consequentialism + deontology; supererogation → pacifism; virtue_ethics → practical_wisdom in bioethical judgment) ALSO deferred to P5-11 — deliberate choice differing from the P5-01b / P5-02b precedents because P5-04a's normative-theory layer is sufficiently dense that authoring those cross-cluster edges in this seed would have produced denser cross-references than within-cluster substructure. `provenance='ai-seed'` everywhere. `graph_version` 7 → 8 in same transaction as the 62 INSERTs. Edge structure: 6-tier layered DAG (T0 applied_ethics; T1 bioethics + environmental_ethics + just_war_theory + business_ethics + technology_ethics; T2 medical_ethics / research_ethics / four_principles_bioethics / anthropocentrism / biocentrism / ecocentrism / climate_ethics / pacifism / ai_ethics; T3 end_of_life_ethics / reproductive_ethics / autonomy_bioethical / beneficence / non_maleficence / justice_bioethical / deep_ecology / animal_ethics / future_generations; T4 informed_consent / sentientism / intergenerational_justice; T5 non_identity_problem). Every edge points lower→higher tier so Kosaraju SCC check confirms acyclicity post-apply. Authored under task P5-04b of `T-PHASE-5` per [`engine/build_readiness/phase_5.md`](build_readiness/phase_5.md). **Apply mechanics (S-0058 chunked-execute_sql + apply_migration-marker pattern continued)**: ~94 KB executable SQL too large for single MCP `apply_migration`; applied via four `execute_sql` calls (UPDATE settings; INSERT 14 nodes — applied_ethics through anthropocentrism; INSERT 14 nodes — biocentrism through ai_ethics; INSERT 34 edges) in FK-safe order, then `apply_migration` with name `0026_seed_ethics_part1` and no-op body recorded the migration name in `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations`. Pre-apply awk-grep escape-bug sweep clean. Live verification post-apply: 188 total nodes, 240 total edges in `paideia-dev`. **Routine-boot-freshness exercised**: routine_boot_freshness.py FF'd 3 commits (eager-claim S-0058, deliverable, close from parallel worktree sharp-clarke-93896d) before reading shared state per [ADR 0052](adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md) — second non-test-fixture exercise; behavior matches docstring contract.

### Added (S-0055 — routine-mode hardening; Issues #12, #13, #14, #15 closed)
- [`engine/adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md`](adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md) — **Three-layer routine-boot hardening**, per Issue #15. Diagnosis correction landed mid-session: the original "concurrent eager-claim race" framing was wrong — the prior session had already closed before the loser started. Actual failure was boot-time staleness. Layers: (1) `routine_boot_freshness.py` mechanical fast-forward (primary; addresses actual S-0054 failure mode); (2) `routine_lock.py` O_EXCL atomic lockfile with stale-after-1h auto-eviction (defense-in-depth per user direction); (3) `routine_eager_claim_recovery.py` mechanically-verified bounded reset on push-rejection (residual). All three hooked into routine-mode-lifecycle Skill steps 0a, 0b, step-8 push-rejection branch, step-11 lock-release.
- [`engine/adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md`](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) — **Mechanism-first-exercise gate**, per Issue #12 + S-0052 health-check Finding A. Sibling to ADR 0040's build-readiness gate; mechanism-triggered (vs phase-triggered). Resolves all four open sub-questions in-band: disjunctive trigger criterion (new session mode / new validator soft-warn category dependent on session-side discipline / new state file boot reads / Consequences spans ≥3 ops docs OR ≥5 tools); same Tier 1/2/3 triage rubric; deliberation lives in this ADR + new ops doc + per-mechanism reports under `engine/build_readiness/`; gate fires once per qualifying mechanism. Cross-cutting ADRs going forward must include a trigger-criterion evaluation block.
- [`engine/operations/mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md`](operations/mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) — **Layer 1 procedure for ADR 0053.** When the gate fires; how to fire the mechanism interactively against real state; how to observe and instrument; how to triage findings; how to author the gate report at `engine/build_readiness/<mechanism>_first_exercise.md`.
- [`engine/tools/_venv_reexec.py`](tools/_venv_reexec.py) — **Auto-reexec helper for psycopg-importing tools**, per Issue #14. `ensure_venv_python(required_module="psycopg")` walks up from the script's directory to find `.venv/bin/python3` (worktree-local first, main-repo fallback — same precedence as `scrub_env.sh`) and `os.execv`'s the venv interpreter when the required module isn't importable. Subtle bug fix during smoke testing: pass the symlink path (not resolved path) as argv[0] so Python uses pyvenv.cfg to bootstrap site-packages — resolving the symlink loads the underlying interpreter without venv site-packages.
- [`engine/tools/audit_archive_structured_fields.py`](tools/audit_archive_structured_fields.py) — **Hard-fail close on missing `outcome_summary_soft_warns`**, per Issue #13. Symmetric in shape to `audit_handoff_dispositions.py`. Pre-commit hook fires on closing commits via `git show :engine/session/archive/S-NNNN.json | python3 ... --from-stdin`. Defends ADR 0042's persistent-warn surface against silent field-absence lapses (S-0043 → S-0047 case study). Optional secondary advisory when field is empty AND session had ≥3 commits.
- [`engine/tools/routine_boot_freshness.py`](tools/routine_boot_freshness.py) — Layer 1 of ADR 0052 fix. Best-effort `git fetch`, then ancestor check, then `git merge --ff-only origin/main` if behind. Diverged HEAD exits 2 (refuse boot).
- [`engine/tools/routine_lock.py`](tools/routine_lock.py) — Layer 2 of ADR 0052 fix. CLI: `acquire | release | check`. Default lockfile at `.claude/routine.lock` (gitignored under `.claude/*`). Stale-after default 1 hour.
- [`engine/tools/routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`](tools/routine_eager_claim_recovery.py) — Layer 3 of ADR 0052 fix. Verifies eager-claim-race shape (one commit ahead, both sides claim same slot) before performing bounded `git reset --hard origin/main`. Whitelisted carve-out to routine-mode destructive-action posture per CLAUDE.md.
- 5 new test files (`test__venv_reexec.py`, `test_audit_archive_structured_fields.py`, `test_routine_boot_freshness.py`, `test_routine_lock.py`, `test_routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`) — 39 new tests total, all passing.

### Added (S-0054 — Phase 5 metaphysics core seed; P5-02a complete)
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0030_seed_metaphysics_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0030_seed_metaphysics_part1.sql) — **third Phase 5 seed migration; first metaphysics file.** 27 nodes + 30 edges covering the four core metaphysics pillars per [phase_5.md](build_readiness/phase_5.md) T1-B. Four clusters: (1) being / ontology (metaphysics, ontology, existence, substance, property, relation, event, abstract_object, concrete_object); (2) identity (numerical_identity, leibniz_law, persistence, endurantism, perdurantism, temporal_parts, ship_of_theseus); (3) causation (causation, humean_regularity_theory, counterfactual_theory_of_causation, causal_powers); (4) time (time, a_theory_of_time, b_theory_of_time, presentism, eternalism, growing_block_theory, mctaggarts_paradox). All 27 nodes `confidence_level=INTERPRETED` (mirrors P5-01a/P5-01b distribution at 100%; phase_5.md T2-B floor satisfied); all 30 edges `pedagogical_prerequisite`. `domain[]` exactly `{metaphysics}` for every node — cross-domain bridges deferred to P5-11. `provenance='ai-seed'` everywhere. `graph_version` 3 → 4 in same transaction as the 57 INSERTs. Authored under task P5-02a of `T-PHASE-5` per [`engine/build_readiness/phase_5.md`](build_readiness/phase_5.md). Migration applied via Supabase MCP `apply_migration`; live verification: 81 total nodes, 102 total edges in `paideia-dev`. Cold-review pass at shutdown matched contract end-to-end (sub-agent verified node/edge counts, single-tag domain[], graph_version=4 everywhere, transaction wrap, all source/target IDs resolve, no cycles, no DDL, no new predicates, granularity-principle adherence, specialized concepts correctly deferred to P5-02b).
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md) — **per-session narrative entry for S-0054.** Documents the four-cluster decomposition, the spine + four-branches + cross-cluster-bridges edge structure, the cross-domain deferrals to P5-11, the `confidence_level` distribution (100% INTERPRETED), the `graph_version` increment 3→4, and the two-commit pattern adoption per S-0053 procedural finding.
- **GitHub Issue #14** (`tech-debt`) — **routine-fired check_target.py / validate.py silently fail when venv not on PATH.** Surfaced at S-0054 boot: bare `python3 engine/tools/check_target.py` resolves to system Python (3.9, no psycopg) and emits "psycopg not available; cannot verify" FAIL on every `migration_applied` criterion — false-FAIL classification that would mark a successfully-completed task as `blocked` at step-10 verification. Fix is sourcing `engine/tools/scrub_env.sh` before invocation, OR (better) auto-reexec under venv Python at the top of the affected scripts. Outside P5-02a's `scope_lock`; filed for the next interactive `/start-engine` session per ADR 0048 routing. User direction: "file the issue for review later."

### Added (S-0051 — Issue #9 fix unblocks P5-01a; Issue #10 boot-staleness check; label optimization)
- **Boot-time worktree-staleness check** in [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) (Issue #10). Runs `git fetch --no-tags --quiet origin main` then `git merge-base --is-ancestor origin/main HEAD`; emits a LOUD attention block to stderr when HEAD is behind origin/main, surfacing the recovery command (`git fetch && git merge --ff-only origin/main`) inline. Status logged to `.claude/logs/session-start.log` as `stale_check=up-to-date|behind-N|fetch-failed|not-a-git-repo|not-run`. Best-effort (network failure exits silently with log line; never blocks). Closes the gap that surfaced at S-0051 boot: a worktree created before a remote update sees stale shared-state files (`register_state.json`, `current.json`, `auto_target.json`) and the AI proceeds on stale truth. Filed Issue #10 then fixed in same session per S-0051 user direction "no more session cascade for every bug — fix it here."
- **Two GitHub Issue label-taxonomy entries with authoring procedures**: `documentation` (doc improvements/bugs/cleanup) and `question` (genuine open questions needing deliberation before action shape clarifies). Both join the existing 6 type labels in [`engine/operations/issue-discipline.md`](operations/issue-discipline.md) "Label taxonomy" table.
- **New "Reactive-only labels" section** in [`engine/operations/issue-discipline.md`](operations/issue-discipline.md) framing `duplicate`, `invalid`, `wontfix` as triage-time-applied (no authoring procedure). Documents the dropping of community labels (`good first issue`, `help wanted`) at S-0051.
- **`count_upstream_bugs` helper + 2 new tests** in [`engine/tools/scan_issue_backlog.py`](tools/scan_issue_backlog.py) + [`engine/tools/test_scan_issue_backlog.py`](tools/test_scan_issue_backlog.py). The helper counts issues tagged BOTH `bug` AND `upstream`; the new format_fyi_line subtracts that from the bug count and surfaces upstream separately. Tests cover the subtraction including floor-at-zero defensive case.
- **Regression test `test_migration_applied_queries_name_column`** in [`engine/tools/test_check_target.py`](tools/test_check_target.py) — mocks `psycopg.connect`, asserts SQL passed to `cursor.execute` references the `name` column with the descriptive id; locks Issue #9's fix.

### Fixed (S-0050 — first Phase 5 routine-mode session)
- **First end-to-end routine-mode work product.** Seed migration applied + ROUTING narrative + commit + push all succeeded under routine-mode discipline (eager-claim, scope-locked work, in-band Issue filing for out-of-scope discovery, blocked-task disposition, HANDOFF entry, shutdown sequence). The pattern is exercised; the verifier bug is the first real discovery the pattern caught.
- **Phase 4 graph validation success criteria.** ROADMAP §4 named two outstanding criteria — `<3s on a 100-node test seed` (28 nodes here, well under 100; runtime well under 3s observed) and `pre-commit hook blocks seed-authoring commits that fail audit` (commit went through cleanly because there were 0 hard-fails; the negative case wasn't exercised but the positive case was). The first Phase 5 seed exercises the audit end-to-end against real seed content for the first time.

### Added (S-0049 — walk-up `.env` loader; Issue #8 closed)
- [`engine/tools/load_env.py`](tools/load_env.py) — **new walk-up `.env` loader.** `find_dotenv` walks up from cwd up to a 10-ancestor depth cap looking for the nearest `.env`; `load_dotenv` parses (reusing `parse_env` from S-0048's [`setup_env.py`](tools/setup_env.py) — no new dep, no duplicate parser) and applies values to `os.environ` for keys not already set (or all if `override=True`); `load_dotenv_walk_up` combines the two as the standard call site for tool main(). Module also has a `__main__` diagnostic that prints the located `.env` and its populated keys.
- [`engine/tools/test_load_env.py`](tools/test_load_env.py) — **14 tests.** `find_dotenv` (start hit / nested dirs / nearest-wins precedence / depth cap / cwd default / none-when-absent), `load_dotenv` (sets missing / preserves pre-set when `override=False` / overrides on `override=True` / skips empty values / ignores comments and blanks), `load_dotenv_walk_up` (no-env empty / idempotent / worktree-shaped tree).

### Changed (S-0049 — walk-up `.env` loader; Issue #8 closed)
- [`engine/tools/check_target.py`](tools/check_target.py) `main()` — calls `load_dotenv_walk_up()` before argparse so `_check_migration_applied` sees `SUPABASE_DB_URL`.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) `main()` — same wiring before argparse so `_read_graph_from_db` sees `SUPABASE_DB_URL` and the graph audit engages.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) graph audit — psycopg `ImportError` flipped from hard-fail to soft-skip (records `graph_audit_skipped` + stderr note). Pre-S-0049 the hard-fail was correct because `SUPABASE_DB_URL` being set was an explicit user commitment to having psycopg. Post-S-0049, the walk-up loader auto-loads the URL in any reachable-`.env` context including pre-commit's system-Python invocation (no psycopg there). Audit-skip is the right disposition for that case; the stderr note flags the gap if a user *intended* the audit.
- [`HANDOFF.md`](../HANDOFF.md) — would-be-S-0049 routine fire's HANDOFF entry gains a `**Resolved:** S-0049 (commit 21285f8)` line per the disposition discipline.

### Fixed (S-0049 — walk-up `.env` loader; Issue #8 closed)
- **GitHub Issue #8 closed.** Backlog 3 → 2 (only upstream MemPalace #1, #2 remain). Live verification: `check_target.py --task-id P5-01a` from this worktree (no local `.env`, `SUPABASE_DB_URL` unset in shell) correctly queried the DB and reported `migration_applied` FAIL with "migration 0011_seed_epistemology_part1 not in schema_migrations" — i.e., URL was loaded via walk-up, DB was queried, migration is correctly absent (Phase 5 hasn't started). `validate.py` ran 30 checks (was 23) — graph audit engaged. Pre-commit hook still works correctly under system Python via the soft-skip path. pytest 576/576 (was 562; +14 new). User can resume `paideia-engine-loop` Routine in Hourly mode.

### Added (S-0048 — GitHub Issues backlog cleanup; 5 issues closed)
- [`engine/tools/check_settings_sync.py`](tools/check_settings_sync.py) — **new pre-commit guard** (per Issue #5). Hard-fails any commit from a worktree where main's `.claude/settings.json` differs from the worktree's tracked copy AND the worktree's copy is not staged for the current commit. Resolves the silent-no-op vector that hit S-0046 (harness redirected the worktree Write to main's copy; `git status` from the worktree saw no diff; close commit shipped without the deliverable). Detects worktree via `git rev-parse --git-common-dir` + `realpath` mirroring the pattern in `engine/tools/scrub_env.sh:67-72`. Silent no-op when not in a worktree or when files match. Exit codes: 0 synced/not-applicable, 1 divergent-not-staged hard-fail, 2 tool error. Wired into `engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit` after the routine-mode scope-check.
- [`engine/tools/test_check_settings_sync.py`](tools/test_check_settings_sync.py) — **12 tests.** Three layers: pure-function (`files_differ`), `main()` integration with monkeypatched helpers (no-conflict / in-sync / divergent-not-staged hard-fails / divergent-staged passes / missing-worktree-file treated-as-divergent), real-git integration (`detect_worktree` + `is_staged` against tmp_path repos with worktree subprocess + a real-worktree end-to-end). All 12 pass under venv Python 3.12 and system Python 3.9.
- [`engine/tools/check_session_conflict.py`](tools/check_session_conflict.py) — **new boot-time guard** (per Issue #3). Detects when `register_state.json` says `current_status: in_progress` before the eager-claim ritual runs. Three dispositions: exit 0 no-conflict (closed/absent or current.json absent or unparseable), exit 1 recent collision (<1h) or ambiguous mid-window (1h–24h), exit 2 stale (>24h, recovery candidate). Configurable windows via `--recent-window-seconds` / `--stale-window-seconds`. Wired into `engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh` (informational; hook always exits 0) and `/start-engine` step 4b + session-build-lifecycle.md step 5b (refusal point for the AI).
- [`engine/tools/test_check_session_conflict.py`](tools/test_check_session_conflict.py) — **16 tests.** Cover `parse_started_at` (Z-suffix, `+00:00`, malformed → None), every `check()` disposition (no-register / closed / in-progress + various age windows / future-dated clock-skew / Z-suffix parsing / custom windows), `main()` integration with `--repo-root` and `--quiet`. Real e2e against in-flight S-0048 confirmed correct identification (14-min-old session as recent collision, exit 1, LOUD surface).
- [`engine/tools/setup_env.py`](tools/setup_env.py) — **new one-time `.env` setup helper** (per Issue #7). Reads `.env.example` to discover canonical keys, reads `.env` to preserve existing values, prompts only for missing/empty keys, validates `SUPABASE_DB_URL` with a real `psycopg.connect()` + `SELECT version()`, writes `.env` atomically (write-tmp + rename) with 0600 permissions. Idempotent — re-running with all values populated prints "all set" and exits. Replaces "user manually pastes the URL into .env once, ever" with a guided one-time setup that validates as it goes; subsequent routine fires read the populated `.env` directly.
- [`engine/tools/test_setup_env.py`](tools/test_setup_env.py) — **15 tests.** Cover `parse_env_example` (simple / no-comments / multi-line comment block), `parse_env` (basic / whitespace-strip / value-with-equals / blank-and-comment-ignored / no-equals-ignored), `write_env_atomic` (round-trip / 0600 permission / overwrite-existing), `determine_blocks` (all-populated short-circuit / missing-key prompts / empty-value-prompts / skipped-value-stays-empty).
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) — **two new boot surfaces.** (1) Concurrent-session collision check: invokes `check_session_conflict.py` after the cadence-trigger surface; surfaces stderr at exit 1/2; hook always exits 0 per its "never blocks" design. (2) `.env` onboarding pointer: emits a LOUD surface when `engine/session/auto_target.json` is present AND `.env` is missing `SUPABASE_DB_URL`, naming the exact `setup_env.py` command. Goes silent the moment `.env` carries the URL. `log_ok` telemetry gains `conflict=<status>` and `env_pointer=<status>` fields.
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) — **new "Editing settings.json from a worktree" subsubsection** under "Harness permission allowlist" documenting the cp procedure that the new pre-commit guard's stderr message points at. The guard is a backstop for any session that forgets the cp.

### Changed (S-0048 — GitHub Issues backlog cleanup; 5 issues closed)
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) — **"Harness permission allowlist" subsection rewritten end-to-end** (per Issue #6). New operational stance: routine sessions run in **Auto** permission mode; project-level mechanical safeguards (`check_routine_scope.py --plan/--staged`, master-plan-integrity, `audit_handoff_dispositions.py`, validate.py soft-warns, eager-claim atomic protocol) are the load-bearing anti-rogue layer. Why the S-0046 allowlist approach didn't generalize: the AI inside a routine session naturally uses compound Bash forms (`cmd1; cmd2`, `cmd && cmd`) and the harness matches the *whole* compound command against patterns rather than the leading prefix — pattern proliferation never converges. New trade-off table enumerating what Auto mode permits vs what each project safeguard prevents (for routine-task work, edits outside scope_lock, master-plan revisions, destructive ops, HANDOFF disposition, gh issue create, arbitrary new Bash). Allowlist stays in `.claude/settings.json` for interactive `/start-engine` sessions where Default + human-in-the-loop adds value. The S-0046 same-commit pairing rule is retired.
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) — **"Mechanical safeguard" subsection flipped from "planned, not yet landed" to "landed at S-0048 per Issue #3"** (per Issue #3 closure). Names `check_session_conflict.py`'s three dispositions and the two wire-points (session-start hook + slash command boot procedure).
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) — **new step 5b** before the eager-claim ritual: run `check_session_conflict.py`, refuse on exit 1 (recent collision or ambiguous mid-window), offer auto-recovery on exit 2 (stale).
- [`.claude/commands/start-engine.md`](../.claude/commands/start-engine.md) — **new step 4b** matching the session-build-lifecycle addition.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) — **new settings.json sync check section** invoking `check_settings_sync.py` after the routine-mode scope-check. Hard-fails commits from a worktree where main vs worktree `.claude/settings.json` differ AND the worktree's copy isn't staged.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — **mechanization-list bullet for "Routine-mode harness permission allowlist" rewritten** to match the Auto-mode-supersedes-allowlist stance per Issue #6.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — **new posture bullet** under "Posture vs machinery" → "postures held by AI discipline" naming the operating policy for context-pressure monitoring (Issue #4 closed as intractable). Live transcript-token measurement is infrastructurally blocked (Claude Code does not expose the in-progress transcript path to hooks); prior-archive telemetry is too noisy a proxy; tiktoken estimates are imprecise even at shutdown. User policy: manually monitor context load during routine review; sessions archived with `transcript_token_pct >= 0.70` get post-hoc review pass.
- [`README.md`](../README.md) — **"Setup for a fresh clone" section** adds the `python3 engine/tools/setup_env.py` step plus dashboard URL guidance (where to find `SUPABASE_DB_URL`, what to do if the dashboard masks the password).
- [`engine/operations/seed-chunked-authoring.md`](operations/seed-chunked-authoring.md) — **new "One-time setup of `SUPABASE_DB_URL`" subsubsection** under "Validator skip behavior" documenting the helper + the dashboard-only nature of the DB password.
- [`.claude/settings.json`](../.claude/settings.json) — **three new allowlist entries** for the new tools (`check_settings_sync.py`, `check_session_conflict.py`, `setup_env.py`).

- **GitHub Issues #3, #4, #5, #6, #7 closed.** Backlog 7 → 2 (only the upstream MemPalace bugs #1, #2 remain awaiting upstream fixes). ### Fixed (S-0047 — Settings.json desync patch; lands S-0046's missing deliverable)
- [`.claude/settings.json`](../.claude/settings.json) — **the actual 60+ pattern allowlist extension committed in git for the first time.** S-0046's close commit (2c5da6c) shipped the companion documentation (routine-mode-operations.md subsection, CLAUDE.md mechanization-list bullet, STATE.md and ENGINE_LOG entries) but missed this file because the harness redirected the in-session Write to main repo's `.claude/settings.json` (where the harness reads from) while git tracked the worktree's stale copy. The desync was invisible to `git status` from the worktree (no diff) and the close commit landed looking complete despite the deliverable being functionally absent from git. S-0047's one-line fix: `cp <main>/.claude/settings.json <worktree>/.claude/settings.json && git add && git commit`. Pairs with the routine-mode-operations.md "Harness permission allowlist" subsection that landed in S-0046 documenting the rule.
- **GitHub Issue #5 filed** per ADR 0048 issue-discipline: `bug` — the systemic gap (harness Write to `.claude/settings.json` from a worktree redirects to main; git tracks the worktree's local copy). Proposes (A) pre-commit hook check that compares main vs worktree settings.json and hard-fails on diff-not-staged, (B) auto-sync on session boot, (C) document the asymmetry in routine-mode-operations.md. Recommendation in Issue body: A + C. Out of S-0047 scope (the fixup is single-deliverable).

### Changed (S-0046 — Routine-mode harness permission allowlist patch)
- [`.claude/settings.json`](../.claude/settings.json) — **`permissions.allow` extended** to cover the routine procedure's complete Bash command surface. Pre-S-0046 the file held only the main-repo lifecycle git commands (FF-merge, push, log, status, rev-parse, fetch, diff). Post-S-0046 it covers: engine python tools (every `engine/tools/*.py` script invokable via `python3` with any args — `check_target`, `check_routine_scope`, `validate`, `scan_context_telemetry`, `audit_handoff_dispositions`, `scan_issue_*`, `scan_orphans`, `health_check`, `probe_*`, `parse_structural_reference`, `audit_side_discoveries`); worktree-side git lifecycle (`add/commit/rm/mv/status/diff/log/rev-parse/fetch/show/ls-files/pull --ff-only origin main/config --get`); test/lint stack (`pytest`, `ruff`, `mypy` direct and via `python3 -m`); GitHub Issues path (`gh issue create/list/view/close/comment` plus `gh label list`); Supabase migration tooling (`supabase db push/migration new/migration list/migration repair`); hook scripts (`bash engine/tools/hooks/*.sh`); shell utilities (`date`, `ls`, `cat` of session files, `head/tail/wc/grep/rg/find . -name`); MemPalace CLI (`mempalace search/status/list-drawers/add-drawer/diary read/diary write`); `source engine/tools/scrub_env.sh`. Closes the S-0044 gap where the foundation shipped a load-bearing assumption ("we'll lean on the allowlist") without authoring the allowlist; the first manual routine fire after S-0045 master plan deadlocked at the boot procedure's very first Bash invocation (`python3 engine/tools/check_target.py` for the target-met check).
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) — **new "Harness permission allowlist" subsection** placed after "Mixing interactive and routine sessions". Documents the executability vs. correctness layer distinction (harness allowlist vs. project-level scope-lock per ADR 0051); the S-0044 lesson; the rule that adding a new Bash invocation to the routine procedure REQUIRES a paired allowlist entry in the same commit; the verification path (manual routine fire + boot procedure walk); the recovery path when a routine deadlocks (deny → identify pattern → patch allowlist → re-fire). Routine UI configuration table updated: "Ask permissions: Default" entry's Notes column now references `.claude/settings.json` (project-scope, tracked) instead of `.claude/settings.local.json` (gitignored).
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — **mechanization-list bullet added for the harness permission allowlist** as the executability layer that complements ADR 0051's scope-lock (correctness layer). Names the same-commit pairing rule.

### Added (S-0045 — Phase 5 master plan; routine-mode dispatches against auto_target.json)
- [`product/adr/0052-phase-5-philosophy-subdomain-decomposition.md`](../product/adr/0052-phase-5-philosophy-subdomain-decomposition.md) — **new product ADR.** Phase 5 decomposes into 9 subject subdomains (epistemology, metaphysics, logic, ethics, political philosophy, aesthetics, philosophy of mind, philosophy of language, philosophy of science) plus 3 operational tasks (service nodes, cross-bridges, closeout). Class-boundary admit-criterion governs future readmission (top-level coverage in SEP/Routledge browse categories AND graph-shape distinctness from existing 9 subdomains AND non-trivial concept inventory at the granularity principle). Out of scope, deferred: philosophy of religion (cosmological-argument-shaped concepts fold into metaphysics for this MVP); history of philosophy as separate subdomain (per ADR 0008, thinkers are not nodes; historical concepts surface across the 9 subdomains via cross-bridges). Adjudication closed material divergence between canonical build_plan/ROADMAP list (6 subjects, missing logic/political/aesthetics) and post-S-0044 STATE.md text (8 subjects, missing philosophy of language and standalone services).
- [`engine/build_readiness/phase_5.md`](build_readiness/phase_5.md) — **new gate report covering full Phase 5 batch.** Authored by S-0045 master plan session per ADR 0040 + ADR 0051 (master plan IS the gate session for Phase 5). 7 Tier 1 entries (subdomain decomposition, task pre-splitting, max_sessions, depends_on graph, cross_domain_dependency deferral, closeout criteria, paused state); 8 Tier 2 entries (migration ranges, confidence_level composition, soft-warn recalibrations, scope_lock shape, criteria shape, depends_on encoding, adversarial reconnaissance, source-acquisition); 7 Tier 3 forward-pointers (rollback verification, cross_domain_dependency predicate, rigor_score calibration, soft-warn thresholds, adversarial-triage prompt template, mid-session context-pressure signal, philosophy of religion readmission). Every Tier 1/2 decision cites source-document line(s) per ADR 0040.
- [`engine/session/auto_target.json`](session/auto_target.json) — **new executable contract.** `target_id: T-PHASE-5`, `goal`, `paused: false`, `max_sessions: 18`, `max_wall_clock_hours: 96`, 16 explicit tasks. Subdomains pre-split at master-plan time per `auto_target.schema.md:149` ("Break work into session-sized tasks"): epistemology core/specialized (P5-01a/b), metaphysics core/specialized (P5-02a/b), ethics metaethics+normative/applied (P5-04a/b), philosophy of mind core/consciousness-specialized (P5-07a/b). Single tasks: logic (P5-03), political philosophy (P5-05), aesthetics (P5-06), philosophy of language (P5-08), philosophy of science (P5-09), service nodes (P5-10), cross-bridges (P5-11), closeout (P5-12). Per-task tight `scope_lock.allowed_paths` matching the migration sub-range plus PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md and ROUTING.md. `criteria` are objective, runnable: `migration_applied` for the first migration in the task's range plus `validate_passes` for subdomain tasks; closeout uses `adr_status` + `file_exists` + `validate_passes`. `depends_on` graph: P5-01a anchor; b-halves depend on their a-halves; subjects parallel-eligible after P5-01a; cross-bridges blocks on all 9 subjects + services; closeout blocks on cross-bridges.

Routine sessions have no live context-pressure detection (CLAUDE.md budget percentages are AI posture, not machinery; `scan_context_telemetry.py` runs only at shutdown; auto-compact fires too late at ~95%). Out of S-0045 scope; routed to backlog. S-0045 engineers around the gap by sizing tasks pre-execution per the schema's discipline.

- [`engine/tools/check_target.py`](tools/check_target.py) — **fix-in-context.** `_check_validate_passes` was treating validate.py exit 1 as fail; per `auto_target.schema.md` (validate_passes section), criterion passes iff zero hard-fails. validate.py main() exits 1 whenever any soft-warn fires; the persistent `issue_collision` soft-warns from open Issues #1/#2/#3/#4 keyword-matching every routine session would have blocked all routine `validate_passes` criteria. Fixed: criterion now passes when validate.py exits 0 OR 1; only exit 2 (hard fails) is fail. Updated docstring explains the three-exit-code semantic.
