### Added (S-0028 — Phase 3 SQL schema implementation)
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0001_users_mirror.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0001_users_mirror.sql) — **new migration.** Creates `public.users` mirror of `auth.users` (id UUID PK, email, created_at) plus `handle_new_auth_user` and `handle_deleted_auth_user` SECURITY DEFINER trigger functions on `auth.users` INSERT and DELETE. RLS enabled with self-select-only policy.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0002_nodes.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0002_nodes.sql) — **new migration.** Creates `public.nodes` per [`product/docs/architecture.md`](../product/docs/architecture.md) "Node Schema": `id TEXT PRIMARY KEY` (slugified human-readable concept names), `confidence_level` and `status` CHECK constraints, two-column rigor-score override, RLS with read-allowed-to-authenticated.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0003_edges.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0003_edges.sql) — **new migration.** Creates `public.edges` per architecture.md "Edge Schema": `id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid()`, `source_id`/`target_id TEXT REFERENCES public.nodes(id)`, `edge_type TEXT` (intentionally unconstrained per architecture.md:182), `weight` and `confidence` CHECK [0,1], `UNIQUE (source_id, target_id, edge_type)`. RLS with read-allowed-to-authenticated.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0004_settings.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0004_settings.sql) — **new migration.** Creates `public.settings` (key TEXT PK, value JSONB) and seeds `('graph_version', '1'::JSONB)` per gate T2-D. RLS service-role-only.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0005_learner_events.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0005_learner_events.sql) — **new migration.** Creates `public.learner_events` event-sourced log per [ADR 0015](adr/../../product/adr/0015-event-sourced-learner-model.md) and [ADR 0026](../product/adr/0026-persistent-learner-storage-structural-not-substantive.md). FK `user_id REFERENCES public.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` per [ADR 0031](../product/adr/0031-erasure-mechanism-and-individual-only-regime.md). Sub-signals stored raw per [ADR 0024](../product/adr/0024-engagement-depth-sub-signals-stored-raw.md). Structured context columns (path_id, source_text_id, session_id) per ADR 0026 + ADR 0031. Table-level CHECK `sub_signals_range_or_null` per gate T2-B. RLS with `user_id = auth.uid()`.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0006_mastery_snapshots.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0006_mastery_snapshots.sql) — **new migration.** Creates `public.mastery_snapshots` cached mastery state per [ADR 0023](../product/adr/0023-engagement-depth-aggregation.md), [ADR 0024](../product/adr/0024-engagement-depth-sub-signals-stored-raw.md), [ADR 0025](../product/adr/0025-historical-maximum-tracking.md). Composite PK (user_id, concept_id), `max_historical_score DEFAULT 0`. Two indexes per gate T2-C. RLS user-isolation.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0007_tension_log.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0007_tension_log.sql) — **new migration.** Creates `public.tension_log` per [`product/docs/self-correction.md`](../product/docs/self-correction.md) + ADR 0026. IMMUTABLE function `tension_log_exchange_summary_valid_v1(jsonb)` enforces v1 vocabularies from [TENSION_VOCABULARY.md](../product/seed-graph/migrations/TENSION_VOCABULARY.md). `user_id` added per ADR 0031 Consequences. RLS user-isolation.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0008_security_hardening.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0008_security_hardening.sql) — **new migration.** Addresses three Supabase advisors against S-0028's authored functions: pin search_path on `tension_log_exchange_summary_valid_v1`; REVOKE EXECUTE on `handle_new_auth_user` and `handle_deleted_auth_user` from PUBLIC, anon, authenticated. Triggers continue firing through the trigger system; only the PostgREST RPC surface is closed.

### Changed (S-0028)
- [`engine/build_readiness/phase_3_sql.md`](build_readiness/phase_3_sql.md) — **gate-report fragments corrected inline** to match canonical design after S-0028 boot surfaced three drifts:
  - **T1-A** — note added that the cascade-from-`auth.users` shape requires both INSERT and DELETE triggers; the original report specified INSERT only. Without the DELETE trigger, account deletion via Supabase Auth removes the `auth.users` row but never deletes the `public.users` mirror, and the `ON DELETE CASCADE` on learner-state FKs never fires (silent ADR 0031 violation).
  - **T2-C** `mastery_snapshots`: `concept_id UUID` → `concept_id TEXT REFERENCES public.nodes(id)`. `nodes.id` is `TEXT` per architecture.md:103 (slugified human-readable concept name with explicit cross-domain readability rationale at architecture.md:124) and self-correction.md:34. The drift was gate-session typo, not a settled design change.
  - **T2-E** `edges`: `source_id`/`target_id UUID` → `TEXT`; `type` → `edge_type`; `provenance JSONB` → `provenance TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'human'`; `evidence JSONB` → `evidence TEXT`. All four diverged from architecture.md "Edge Schema" (the design source per STATE.md "translating product/docs/architecture.md ... into live tables"); S-0028 aligned the gate fragment with the design doc.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md) — **per-session narrative** for S-0028 added documenting all 8 migrations, the gate-report drift corrections, and the downgraded rollback verification (Supabase development branches incur cost; per auto-mode posture, branch creation deferred to explicit user confirmation; rollback proof reduced to "migrations applied cleanly the first time" plus the live-schema verification via `list_tables` / `execute_sql` / `get_advisors`; forward-pointer for the next gate exercise / Phase 4 to set up local Supabase CLI for proper rollback verification).
- **Validator clean.** [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py): 11 checks, **0 hard-fails, 0 soft-warns** at session close. SQL-gates clean per migration: 4 gates (transaction-wrap, CASCADE, RLS-enable, enum-CHECK), 0 hard-fails on each of 8 files. Pytest 56/56 passing. Post-apply Supabase security advisor returned only the Supabase-internal `rls_auto_enable` finding (out of project scope).

### Added (S-0027 — Build-readiness gate protocol + universal expression contract; Phase 3 SQL gate exercise)
- [`engine/adr/0039-universal-expression-contract-across-ai-authoring-patterns.md`](adr/0039-universal-expression-contract-across-ai-authoring-patterns.md) — **new ADR.** Generalizes [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md)'s three-layer posture (Layer 1 contract-first prose, Layer 2 mechanical gates, Layer 3 cold-context review) from Python-only to every AI authoring pattern. Decision: every pattern requires Layer 1 + at least one of L2/L3. Pre-existing pattern-specific contracts ([ADR 0027](../product/adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md), [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md), [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md)) are pre-existing instantiations and remain in force. New AI authoring patterns must declare layer instantiation before any artifact is authored under them ("no row, no authoring"); the build-readiness gate ([ADR 0040](adr/0040-build-readiness-gate-before-substantive-build-sessions.md)) enforces the discipline structurally.
- [`engine/adr/0040-build-readiness-gate-before-substantive-build-sessions.md`](adr/0040-build-readiness-gate-before-substantive-build-sessions.md) — **new ADR.** Commits the project to a halting discipline: every substantive build session is preceded by a gate session whose deliverable is a build-readiness report at `engine/build_readiness/<phase>_<chunk>.md`. Build sessions read the report at boot and halt on absence-or-unresolved-Tier-1. Gate sessions are conversational by default — the AI surfaces decisions and the user directs resolution before authoring begins. The gate compensates for a session-level analog of compound-drift: a build session that begins with unresolved Tier 1 decisions, improvises resolutions, and produces internally coherent artifacts that pass mechanical gates and cold review because both layers check artifact-vs-contract alignment, not contract-vs-reality alignment. The gate inserts a halting checkpoint *before* the contract is authored.
- [`engine/operations/expression-contract-instantiation.md`](operations/expression-contract-instantiation.md) — **new operational surface.** [ADR 0039](adr/0039-universal-expression-contract-across-ai-authoring-patterns.md)'s working document. Per-pattern instantiation table (prose/learner-facing, prose/inward, Python/engine, SQL/migrations, plus TBD rows for TS/teaching-layer, YAML/config, shell/tooling, outward/UI text). Each row names the Layer 1 source-of-truth, Layer 2 gate, Layer 3 review trigger, scope path, and citing ADR.
- [`engine/operations/migration-discipline.md`](operations/migration-discipline.md) — **new Layer 1 source-of-truth for SQL/migrations row.** Sister to [`code-discipline.md`](operations/code-discipline.md) and [`document-voice.md`](operations/document-voice.md). Names per-migration contract block shape (purpose, preconditions, postconditions, invariants, non-responsibilities, cross-cutting decisions), file naming convention (`NNNN_<table_or_purpose>.sql`), transaction wrap, CASCADE on FKs to `users(id)`, RLS-enable on `public.*` tables, CHECK constraint shape on enum-modeled TEXT columns, idempotency, rollback authorship, cold-review prompt template.
- [`engine/operations/build-readiness-gate.md`](operations/build-readiness-gate.md) — **new operational surface.** [ADR 0040](adr/0040-build-readiness-gate-before-substantive-build-sessions.md)'s working document. Gate procedure (read build_plan chunk, launch up to three Explore agents in parallel, triage Tier 1/2/3, resolve Tier 1 with user, author resolution artifacts, write the report, update STATE.md), build-readiness report template, worked example (Phase 3 SQL), failure-modes-the-gate-prevents and failure-modes-the-gate-introduces (honest accounting), amendment discipline.
- [`engine/build_readiness/`](build_readiness/) — **new directory.** Home for build-readiness reports authored by gate sessions. README scaffolds the contract (one report per substantive build session, lifecycle, no-retroactive-edits rule); first occupant is `phase_3_sql.md` from S-0027's gate exercise.
- [`engine/build_readiness/phase_3_sql.md`](build_readiness/phase_3_sql.md) — **new report.** Phase 3 SQL build-readiness report authored by S-0027 for S-0028. Tier 1 resolutions (auth model = local users mirror per ADR 0031 amendment; RLS posture = on with v1 policies; JSONB vocabularies = TENSION_VOCABULARY.md authored; universal contract per ADR 0039; gate protocol per ADR 0040). Tier 2 decisions (CHECK expressions for confidence_level/status/interaction_type/tension_type, sub-signal range CHECK on learner_events, mastery_snapshots full schema with computed_at, settings.graph_version initialization, edges PK + UNIQUE(source,target,type), session_id opaqueness, migration directory location, rollback test sequence). Tier 3 forward pointers (superseded_by remapping → Phase 6, mastery formula version acceptable, ENGINE_LOG vs Supabase migration version coordination resolved this session, cold-review SQL extension resolved this session, backup tag cut this session, health-check cadence proximity, validate_graph stub).
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/TENSION_VOCABULARY.md`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/TENSION_VOCABULARY.md) — **new file.** v1 enum vocabularies for `tension_log.exchange_summary` JSONB fields per [ADR 0026](../product/adr/0026-persistent-learner-storage-structural-not-substantive.md) sub-decision (1) deferral. Three enums: `teaching_moves_tried` (10 values: direct_explanation, concrete_example, analogy, decomposition, prerequisite_check, restatement, socratic_question, contrast_pair, redirect_to_source, pause_and_reframe), `friction_type` (10 values: prerequisite_gap, formula_vs_grounding, source_register_mismatch, terminology_drift, aliasing_confusion, cross_domain_transfer_block, cognitive_overload, motivation_gap, false_mastery, unexpected_ease), `suggested_review_focus` (7 enum values + NULL). Phase 3 migration consumes as JSONB shape constraints; Phase 6 batch review may refine under ADR 0026's amendment discipline.
- [`engine/tools/test_validate.py`](tools/test_validate.py) — **18 new tests** for `validate_sql_gates` covering empty file list, clean migration, missing BEGIN, missing COMMIT, END-keyword acceptance, missing CASCADE on FK to users(id), CASCADE on unqualified users(id), comment-stripping ignores REFERENCES inside comments, missing RLS-enable, unqualified ALTER TABLE accepted, missing CHECK on enum columns, confidence_level CHECK requirement and acceptance, unreadable file failure, multi-file aggregation, plus three `--sql-gates` CLI tests. 56 tests total, all passing.
- Backup tag `pre-phase-3-v0.0.1` cut at commit `36b0907` (S-0026 close). Mirrors the `pre-foundation-v0.0.0` pattern; file-level retrieval via `git show pre-phase-3-v0.0.1:<path>` is the legitimate use. Pushed to origin.

### Changed (S-0027)
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) — **`validate_sql_gates(files: list[Path])` added** implementing Layer 2 of [ADR 0039](adr/0039-universal-expression-contract-across-ai-authoring-patterns.md) for the SQL/migrations pattern. Four gates per file: transaction-wrap (BEGIN/COMMIT or BEGIN/END envelope), CASCADE-present (every FK to `(public.)?users(id)` ends in `ON DELETE CASCADE`), RLS-enabled (every `CREATE TABLE` in `public.*` paired with `ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY`), enum-CHECK (every column declared with a name in `SQL_ENUM_COLUMNS` and TEXT/VARCHAR type carries `CHECK (... IN (...))`). Helper `_strip_sql_line_comments` strips `--` line comments before checks so contract-block keywords don't produce false positives. `main()` extended with `--sql-gates` flag (mutually exclusive with `--code-gates`); module docstring updated to name three responsibility families (repo-structure + code-gates + SQL-gates). Per-function contract blocks under [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md) discipline; `mypy --strict` plus `ruff` clean.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) — **SQL-gates branch added** parallel to the existing code-gates branch. Detects staged `.sql` files under `product/seed-graph/migrations/` via `git diff --cached --name-only --diff-filter=ACMR | grep -E '^product/seed-graph/migrations/.*\.sql$'`; when any are present, invokes `python3 engine/tools/validate.py --sql-gates --files <those>` and blocks the commit on hard-fail.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — **step 3 cold-review pass widened.** Trigger condition now covers SQL under `product/seed-graph/migrations/` in addition to Python under `engine/`. Step 5 ENGINE_LOG section gains a paragraph on migration-version coordination ("ENGINE_LOG records session-level filenames; Supabase migration version tracking is separate and automatic"). Recovery section step 1 widened symmetrically.
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) — **boot procedure step 5 added.** Substantive build sessions read `engine/build_readiness/<phase>_<chunk>.md` at boot. If absent, the session converts to a gate session; if present with unresolved Tier 1 items, the session halts and escalates. Operational sessions skip the step. Original step 5 (slot claim) renumbered to 6; step 6 (substantive work) to 7. Step 7 also names the build session's posture toward the gate report (canonical decision-of-record; in-flight surprises classify as routine judgment / escalation candidate / gate-under-specification signal).
- [`product/adr/0031-erasure-mechanism-and-individual-only-regime.md`](../product/adr/0031-erasure-mechanism-and-individual-only-regime.md) — **Consequences amended** to pin the cascade FK target shape: local `public.users` table mirrors `auth.users` via trigger; app-schema FKs target `public.users(id)` with `ON DELETE CASCADE`; account deletion deletes the `auth.users` row, which cascades through the trigger to `public.users`, which cascades declaratively through every learner-state row. Refinement under existing ADR's amendment posture (cascade-discipline principle unchanged); no superseding ADR.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md) — **moved from `supabase/migrations/`** via `git mv`. Content unchanged.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md) — **moved from `supabase/migrations/`** via `git mv`. Title updated to reflect new path; preamble rewritten to point at `phase_3_sql.md` for the directory-location decision; `graph_version` increment contract added (Phase 5 sessions read current value, increment, write to all new nodes/edges in one transaction; Phase 3 schema migrations initialize at 1 only).
- `supabase/` placeholder removed — `rmdir supabase/migrations supabase` after the two `git mv`s.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) — index rows added for ADR 0039 and ADR 0040; engine collection grows from 5 to 7 ADRs (full project: 40, partitioned 7 engine + 33 product).
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — Topical pointers gain entries for `migration-discipline.md`, `expression-contract-instantiation.md`, `build-readiness-gate.md`.
- [`ROADMAP.md`](../ROADMAP.md) — Phase 2 entry extended with the build-readiness gate machinery; Phase 3 entry annotated as gated by `engine/build_readiness/phase_3_sql.md`. Phase 3 success criteria expanded to name the report's Tier 2 decisions and the rollback-test verification sequence.
- **Validator clean.** [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py): 11 checks, **0 hard-fails, 0 soft-warns** at session close. Code-gates clean: 5 gates, 0 hard-fails. Pytest 56/56 passing. SQL-gates exercised on test fixtures via the pytest suite; first real exercise lands at S-0028 against authored migrations.

### Added (S-0026 — Code expression contract for AI-authored code per [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md))
- [`engine/adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md`](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md) — **new ADR.** Third project expression contract, sibling to [ADR 0027](../product/adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md) (rendering policy for learner-facing prose) and [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md) (inward-facing documents). Targets the compound-drift failure mode that prose-style discipline cannot catch: a small wrong premise built upon by internally-consistent code that passes tests authored against the same premise. Three layers: (1) contract-first prose — docstring contract per function/class, ADR for module-level decisions; (2) mechanical gates — pre-commit gates any staged Python file under engine/ on `ruff check` + `ruff format --check` + `mypy --strict` + test-presence + `pytest`, hard-fail uniformly; (3) cold-context review pass at session shutdown — sub-agent with no session memory reads the diff against contract blocks, findings to `outcome_summary`. Amendment asymmetry follows [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md)'s pattern: refinements within each layer are ENGINE_LOG-tracked (no new ADR); restructuring or removing a layer requires superseding ADR.
- [`engine/operations/code-discipline.md`](operations/code-discipline.md) — **new operational surface.** [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md)'s working document. Carries the contract-block authoring guidance, worked examples (good and bad function-scope contracts, module-level via ADR), the gate-stack invocation commands, the cold-review prompt template, scope (governed / exempt / future product code), and amendment discipline. Sibling tool to [`engine/operations/document-voice.md`](operations/document-voice.md), separately scoped to code.
- [`engine/tools/requirements.txt`](tools/requirements.txt) — **new file.** Engine-tool dependencies declared (`ruff>=0.4`, `mypy>=1.10`, `pytest>=8.0`). Install with `pip install -r engine/tools/requirements.txt`.
- [`engine/tools/test_validate.py`](tools/test_validate.py) — **new file.** Pytest suite for [`validate.py`](tools/validate.py): 38 tests covering `ValidationResult` per-method behavior plus merge semantics; `validate_repo_structure` across all 11 check categories (hard-fail and soft-warn paths); `validate_code_gates` across empty/clean/lint/mypy/missing-test/test-file/nested-test paths; the `validate_graph` stub; telemetry helpers (`session_id_from_current`, `append_history` including OSError swallowing); and `main()` exit-code mapping in both modes. Filesystem isolation via `tmp_path` + `monkeypatch`; subprocess-based gate tests exercise real `ruff` / `mypy` / `pytest` rather than mocks.

### Changed (S-0026)
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) — **retrofitted under [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md).** Module-level plus per-function contract blocks name purpose, inputs (with preconditions), outputs (with postconditions and explicit non-claims), edge cases, exceptions, and non-responsibilities. New `validate_code_gates(files: list[Path])` implements Layer 2 — invokes `ruff check`, `ruff format --check`, `mypy --strict`, test_presence, and `pytest` as subprocesses against the named files; hard-fails uniformly. `main()` extended with `--code-gates` and `--files` flags (mutually exclusive with the default repo-structure mode). Removed unused `import os`. `mypy --strict` plus `ruff` clean. The validator binds to its own gates from this session forward; no grandfathering.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) — **gates wired.** New code-gates branch runs after the existing repo-structure `validate.py` call. Detects staged Python files under engine/ via `git diff --cached --name-only --diff-filter=ACMR | grep -E '^engine/.*\.py$'`; when any are present, invokes `python3 engine/tools/validate.py --code-gates --files <those>` and blocks the commit on hard-fail (exit 2). Soft-warns are not used at this layer per [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md).
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — **new step 3 (cold-review pass), steps 4–8 renumbered.** Sessions that modified tracked Python under engine/ launch a sub-agent with no session context to read each modified file's contract block against the implementation; findings record in `outcome_summary` distinguishing addressed-in-session from deferred-to-follow-up. Sessions that authored prose only skip the step. Recovery section's step references updated.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) — Topical pointers gains the `code-discipline.md` entry between `adr-authoring.md` and `health-check.md`.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) — index row added for [ADR 0038](adr/0038-expression-contract-for-ai-authored-code.md); the engine collection grows from 4 to 5 ADRs (full project: 38, partitioned 5 engine + 33 product).
- [`engine/operations/README.md`](operations/README.md) — Decisions-and-review section gains the `code-discipline.md` pointer.
- **Cold-review pass on this session's Python diff** ([`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) and [`engine/tools/test_validate.py`](tools/test_validate.py)): both files match contract — no drift detected. The mechanism's first exercise lands clean; refinement under load expected at Phase 4 graph-construction work.
- **Validator clean.** [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py): 11 checks, **0 hard-fails, 0 soft-warns** at session close. Code-gates clean: 5 gates (ruff_check, ruff_format, mypy, test_presence, pytest), 0 hard-fails. Pytest 38/38 passing.

### Changed (S-0025 — Engine/product migration cross-reference sweep, S-0024 continuation)
- [`product/docs/CROSS_REFERENCES.md`](../product/docs/CROSS_REFERENCES.md) — **rewritten with partition-aware paths.** The 15 `cross_reference_broken` soft-warns from S-0024 close all stemmed from this file's relative-path geometry shifting one level deeper post-partition. Hrefs rebased: root files reached via `../../ROADMAP.md` etc. (one extra `../`), engine-side targets reached via `../../engine/…` (across the wall), product-side targets via `../adr/…` or sibling-relative. Display labels updated to name partition-aware locations explicitly. Phase 4 → 5 boundary check rewritten to point at `product/seed-graph/migrations/PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md` and `product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md` (the post-partition Phase 3 destination per `build_plan/P_1_sql_schema.md`).
- **Asymmetry decision: `product/docs/CROSS_REFERENCES.md` stays product-side as the single change-propagation index spanning both subtrees.** ADR 0037 left the stay-vs-split question open; settled in this session. The bulk of cross-references are product-product (commitment chains, sibling docs); the procedural-dependencies section is four entries — too thin to justify a parallel `engine/CROSS_REFERENCES.md` plus validator support. [`engine/operations/README.md`](operations/README.md) already serves as the engine procedural index by topic; CROSS_REFERENCES.md fills the change-propagation-dependency role. Engine-side targets reach across the wall via `../../engine/...`. The asymmetry is tolerable: the file lives under product/docs/ because most consumers live there, but it spans the whole tree because dependencies legitimately cross the wall.
- **Bulk partition-aware sweep across the migrated tree.** Mechanical mapper applied: `adr/0NNN-*.md` → `engine/adr/...` (N ∈ {0016, 0022, 0036, 0037}) else `product/adr/...`; `docs/operations/...md` → `engine/operations/...md`; `docs/X.md` → `product/docs/X.md`; `STATE.md` / `ENGINE_LOG.md` → `engine/...`; `CHANGELOG.md` → `product/CHANGELOG.md`; `AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md` → `product/AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md`; `tools/X` / `session/X` → `engine/tools/X` / `engine/session/X`; `ROADMAP.md` / `README.md` / `CLAUDE.md` etc. → unchanged target with relative-climb adjustment for files that moved deeper. Each link rewritten as a file-relative href from its source location; same-directory ADR sibling references that crossed the partition (e.g., `engine/adr/0036` referencing sibling `0027-…md` when 0027 lives in `product/adr/`) repaired via the ADR-number rule. **356 links repaired across 38 files** in two mapper passes; 8 hand-fixed cases for residuals the mapper could not generalize.
- **Hand-fixed cases.** [`build_plan/00_session_schedule.md`](../build_plan/00_session_schedule.md): `product/docs/ui-architecture.md` link rebased to `../product/docs/...`. [`build_plan/P_4_seed_graph_build.md`](../build_plan/P_4_seed_graph_build.md), [`build_plan/P_5_retrieval_mastery_decisions.md`](../build_plan/P_5_retrieval_mastery_decisions.md): forward-pointing references to `product/seed-graph/migrations/` (PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md, ROUTING.md, the directory itself) converted from markdown links to inline-code path mentions, since the directory does not exist until Phase 3 (`P_1`) populates it; the inward-doc voice contract reads markdown links as a claim that the target exists. ### Changed (S-0024 — Engine/product folder migration per [ADR 0037](adr/0037-engine-product-wall-and-changelog-rename.md), structural batch)
- **Repo restructured into `engine/` and `product/` subtrees per [ADR 0037](adr/0037-engine-product-wall-and-changelog-rename.md).** 111 files renamed/created/modified in one structural commit. Engine subtree: `engine/operations/` (← `docs/operations/`, 14 procedural docs), `engine/tools/` (← `tools/`, validators + hooks + setup + telemetry), `engine/session/` (← `session/`, register + current + 23-entry archive), `engine/STATE.md` (← `STATE.md`), `engine/ENGINE_LOG.md` (← `ENGINE_LOG.md`), `engine/adr/` (4 ADRs: 0016, 0022, 0036, 0037). Product subtree: `product/adr/` (33 ADRs — everything in `adr/` minus the 4 engine ADRs), `product/docs/` (← `docs/` minus `operations/`), `product/AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md`, `product/CHANGELOG.md` (the reserved stub). Stays at root: `CLAUDE.md`, `README.md`, `ROADMAP.md`, `HANDOFF.md`, `SECURITY.md`, `LICENSE`, `build_plan/`, `.claude/`, `.git/`, `.gitignore`, `.mcp.json`, `.env*`. `supabase/` stays at root pending [`build_plan/P_1_sql_schema.md`](../build_plan/P_1_sql_schema.md)'s in-session decision per Phase 3.
- [`engine/adr/0037-engine-product-wall-and-changelog-rename.md`](adr/0037-engine-product-wall-and-changelog-rename.md) — **light-revised in checkpoint A.** Edge-case (c) extended: "`.claude/` and `CLAUDE.md` stay at root because Claude Code expects them there." Rationale spelled out in-place: Claude Code's auto-load walks ancestor directories from cwd UP, not into subdirectories; subdirectory `CLAUDE.md` files load lazily only when files inside that subtree are accessed; a naive `engine/CLAUDE.md` would break the load-bearing boot ceremony. The wall this ADR commits to is conceptual — partition by what kind of artifact, not a physical-purity test that every engine artifact must live under `engine/`. `engine/CLAUDE.md` removed from the proposed-shape diagram; `CLAUDE.md` joins the explicit root-level list. Status remains `Accepted` (clarifying revision, not supersession).
- [`build_plan/M_partition_migration.md`](../build_plan/M_partition_migration.md) — **light-revised in checkpoint A.** Risk #5 ("CLAUDE.md auto-load behavior") rewritten: the resolution is "stays at root" per ADR 0037 edge-case (c); the previously-enumerated mitigations (root symlink, thin pointer, `cd engine/` at boot, `@engine/CLAUDE.md` import) are obviated.
- **ADR partition (4 engine, 33 product).** Engine ADRs file under `engine/adr/`: [ADR 0016](adr/0016-graph-construction-needs-live-validation.md) (graph validation infrastructure — load-bearing reader is `engine/tools/validate.py`'s graph audit), [ADR 0022](adr/0022-periodic-project-health-checks.md) (project audits — load-bearing reader is the build-apparatus health-check cadence), [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md) (inward-doc voice contract — governs engine-internal documentation), [ADR 0037](adr/0037-engine-product-wall-and-changelog-rename.md) (the partition itself). Product ADRs file under `product/adr/`: every other ADR (0001–0015, 0017–0021, 0023–0035), spanning pedagogy commitments (0001–0012), product architecture (0013–0021 minus 0016), Phase 1 Contract Lock decisions (0023–0032), Phase 1.5 Mission Realignment decisions (0033–0035). Edge cases settled per the criterion in [`build_plan/M_partition_migration.md`](../build_plan/M_partition_migration.md): [ADR 0014](../product/adr/0014-sonnet-teaches-opus-reviews.md) files product (Sonnet/Opus is product-runtime architecture, not engine machinery); [ADR 0017](../product/adr/0017-postgres-recursive-ctes-over-owl-rdf.md) files product (database schema choice for the product's data layer); [ADR 0027](../product/adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md) and [ADR 0028](../product/adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md) file product per ADR 0037 edge-case (a) explicit (consumer-of-record is learner-facing prose).

### Worktree-shared symlink note (S-0024)

The pre-commit symlink retarget affects all worktrees in this clone (24 active at S-0024 close per the `git worktree list`). Worktrees on pre-migration branches will have a dangling hook target until they merge or rebase the migration commit; their commits will succeed without validator enforcement (git silently skips missing hooks) until they pull. This is acceptable for the personal-project posture but worth noting for any session that reuses an old worktree without merging first.

### Added (S-0020 — Phase 1.5 → Phase 2 bridge: machinery hardening, Tier 2 of approved adversarial-analysis plan)
- [`tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh`](tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh) (new file, tracked, executable) — **A2 MemPalace capture-hook wrapper.** Wraps `mempalace hook run` so capture failures (binary missing, daemon down, capture errored) route to a session-visible log instead of failing silently. Pass-through args (`--hook <stop|precompact> --harness <name>`) and stdin (the harness JSON event payload). Captures `mempalace`'s exit code and stderr, writes a single timestamped `OK` or `FAIL` line to `.claude/logs/mempalace-hook.log`, then exits 0 to the harness regardless of the inner exit code — the log carries the truth, the wrapper never blocks the session. Sentinel env var `PAIDEIA_MEMPALACE_HOOK_FORCE_FAIL=1` synthesizes a failure for verification testing without invoking the real binary; never set in production. Repo-root resolution prefers `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` and falls back to script-location resolution. Manual failure test confirmed: sentinel produced the FAIL log line and harness-side exit 0; subsequent run without the sentinel removed; clean state restored before commit. The log path is gitignored under the existing `.claude/*` rule (per-clone state); no `.gitignore` change needed.
- [`docs/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](docs/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) — new **MemPalace capture-hook failure log** subsection inside the existing `## Recovery` section. Names the boot-time check (`test -s .claude/logs/mempalace-hook.log && cat …`), the acknowledgment-by-truncation procedure (`: > .claude/logs/mempalace-hook.log`), and the most common failure modes (binary not in harness PATH; daemon not running). Cross-references `mempalace-operations.md`. The boot-recovery hint addresses the brief's note that without surfacing, capture failures could persist silently across sessions.
- [`tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) — **B4 ADR-index/file consistency check.** New tenth structural-validation check (`adr_index_consistency`) added to `validate_repo_structure()` immediately after `adr_status`. Parses `adr/README.md`'s per-phase tables (rows of the form `| [NNNN](NNNN-...md) | Title | Status |`) into a `{NNNN: status_text}` map via a single-line regex covering all per-phase sections; for each `adr/NNNN-*.md` file emits the new soft-warn category `adr_index_inconsistent` either when the ADR is not referenced in the index (most common case: a new ADR authored without the index update) or when the ADR file's `Status:` core keyword (Accepted / Superseded / Deprecated / Proposed) differs from the index's status column for that ADR. Status comparison normalizes around the four core keywords rather than literal-equality matching so markdown-link decoration in the status column (e.g., `Superseded by [ADR 0035](...)`) does not produce false positives. Soft-warn rather than hard-fail per the plan's recommendation: the index is human-curated and tolerates formatting variation; false positives should refine the check. Manual test: a throwaway `adr/9999-test-missing-from-index.md` with a Status field but no index entry produced exit 1 with one `adr_index_inconsistent` warn naming the file; deletion restored exit 0 / 0 hard-fails / 0 soft-warns.
- [`docs/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](docs/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) — new `adr_index_inconsistent` soft-warn category documented alongside `adr_missing_status`. Names both failure modes (missing-from-index, status-keyword-mismatch); names the recovery (add the index row, or align Status); names the false-positive policy (refine the check rather than paper over). Marked active from S-0020 onward.

### Added (S-0019 — Phase 1.5 → Phase 2 bridge: machinery hardening, Tier 1 of approved adversarial-analysis plan)
- [`docs/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](docs/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) — New `## Recovery` section with two procedures. **Eager-claim race resolution** (concurrent slot collision: fetch origin/main, hard-reset to upstream, re-claim against the peer-bumped next_id; the boot rule is *claim first, work second*, so destruction is bounded — only the local claim commit is lost; no substantive work is in flight). The mechanism's collision resistance is in place but not stress-tested by an actual concurrent collision; first real exercise will likely come during Phase 5 parallel seed-graph build. **Pre-commit hook symlink** procedure for fresh clones or broken symlink targets (the hook lives at `tools/hooks/pre-commit` tracked; the parent repo's `.git/hooks/pre-commit` symlinks to it via relative `../../tools/hooks/pre-commit`; worktrees share the parent's `.git/hooks/` directory, so one symlink covers every worktree). Restore command plus verification step.
- [`docs/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](docs/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) — New `## Recovery (interrupted shutdown)` section enumerating four observable mid-shutdown states (halted before archive; halted between archive and final commit; halted after final commit before FF + push; split state) with per-state recovery paths. Split-state reconciliation routes through [`docs/operations/escalation-criteria.md`](docs/operations/escalation-criteria.md) when unclear. Recovery procedure documented for completeness; not yet exercised on a real interrupted close.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](CLAUDE.md) `## First-session reading order` — new top-level section naming the four-doc cold-start reading priority ([`session-build-lifecycle.md`](docs/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md), [`session-shutdown-sequence.md`](docs/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md), [`escalation-criteria.md`](docs/operations/escalation-criteria.md), [`tools-validate-interpretation.md`](docs/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md)); other operations docs are defer-on-demand. Complements the existing `## Topical pointers` section (pointers answer "what's available," reading order answers "what must I read first").
- [`CLAUDE.md`](CLAUDE.md) `### Posture vs machinery` — new subsection in Standing rules naming three rules held by AI discipline, not validator/hook enforcement: the **pushback rule** (no audit trail), **two-layer decision recording** (`tools/validate.py` does not check whether settled decisions land in MemPalace alongside their ADR), and **startup ceremony order** (judgment, not gated). The choice is deliberate; the cost is silent drift if discipline lapses; the mitigation is awareness so a session does not mistake the absence of an alarm for the presence of compliance.
- [`docs/tensions.md`](docs/tensions.md) — **OQ-OUTWARD-VOICE** entry added. The third expression-contract gap that neither [ADR 0027](adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md) (Sonnet's teaching prose) nor [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md) (inward-facing project documentation) covers: UI labels, button text, error messages, learner-facing help text, public README, marketing copy, App Store description, learner-visible CHANGELOG entries. Decide-before Phase 7 (the earliest plausible moment such a surface ships); decision shape is a kindred-tool, separately-scoped third contract per the pattern [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md) names. Surfaced by the pre-Phase-2 adversarial machinery audit; logged here so the gap is visible to any future session that touches a learner-facing surface, well before Phase 7.

Scope: governed (`docs/`, root-level project files, ADRs in non-Superseded status, `AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md`); exempt (`STATE.md`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `session/archive/*`, ADRs in `Superseded` status, `docs/tensions.md` resolved entries). Posture (governed inward documents describe present truth in present-tense declarative prose), voice (cross-references bibliographic at end-of-section pointers, not parenthetical commentary on each assertion; "the reader does not need to know what the document used to say"), where-the-trace-lives section cross-linking the four-layer system, worked example (`docs/MISSION.md` opening blockquote rewrite — annotation positively explains what the rewrite does, with the before-version's failure surfacing as instructive contrast inside the worked example rather than as a prohibition section of its own), scope (governed/exempt with `ROADMAP.md` three-speech-acts handling), amendment discipline (refinements CHANGELOG-tracked; posture changes require superseding ADR). Mirrors the [`AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md`](AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md) ↔ [ADR 0027](adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md) separation: the contract document is the working surface, the ADR is the citable contract.
- MemPalace decision drawer for ADR 0036 filed: `drawer_paideia_general_89eaa4e70c1b0581422a8381` (wing `paideia`, room `general`). Carries the verbatim conversational story including the user's two-stage course-correction on framing — first that "expression contract" applies in both directions ("The meaning is the same. Expression contract defines how the AI expresses itself. Be it internally or externally"), then sharpening that "kindred tools, separately scoped" is the correct frame, not "facets of one contract" ("No, an 'expression contract' is a tool that lets an AI voice be constrained. How that tool is used does not make all uses conjoined"). Pattern lessons recorded for future sessions: distinguish "expression contract = X" (definition of category) from "X = the project's expression contract" (claim of identity/composition); a two-stage user correction is itself useful telemetry when an AI over-reads a definition into a structural claim.

Two new bullets in **Forbidden tokens** section, placed between `Mastery verification mechanic` and `Self-reference as machinery`: **Globe / spatial-traversal metaphors** (`globe`, `world` in the sense of "the world of philosophy" or "knowledge as a world", `map`, `territory`, `exploration` in the sense of spatial wandering, `navigate` in the sense of moving across a spatial surface, `journey`, `terrain`, `landscape of knowledge`, framings that present learning as game-world traversal or character-on-map movement; with surviving-tokens callout for *domain*, *field*, *area of inquiry* as abstract category language) and **Reward / visualization language** (`trophy`, `glow`, `mastery glow`, `tendril`, `colored trail`, `badge`, `achievement`, `you've unlocked`, `new territory unlocked`, `lights up`, `illuminates`, congratulatory framing for completion; with directive to surface bridges in plain prose, not as reward events). **Worked example annotations extended**: two new bullets in "Note what this output does and does not do" cover the new categories; a second failing-version example added illustrating reward-flavored / traversal-flavored failure (`You've unlocked the categorical imperative — this is a major node on your path through Kant's ethics. ... new territory in moral philosophy opens up and you'll see tendrils connecting to political philosophy ...`) followed by an acceptable rephrasing showing how to put bridge-surfacing-in-context into prose without reward language. Header attribution and trailing attribution updated to record the S-0016 extension. Phase 7 success criterion (zero forbidden-token leakage on 10 random concept queries) now covers the broader category set without changing its discipline.

### Added (S-0015 — Phase 1.5.3: Multi-platform Apple expansion + Phase 9 rewrite)
- [`adr/0035-multi-platform-apple-expansion.md`](adr/0035-multi-platform-apple-expansion.md) — Multi-platform Apple expansion; iPhone + iPad first-class via SwiftUI, Mac via Designed-for-iPad. **Supersedes [ADR 0032](adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md).** Six binding commitments — five restate verbatim from [ADR 0032](adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md), one broadens. Commitment 1 (broadened): *Apple platforms via App Store. iPhone + iPad first-class via a single SwiftUI codebase. Mac via Designed-for-iPad opt-in with modest keyboard/menu polish. No Android, no web app, no native AppKit/Catalyst Mac app.* Mac polish target is *modest, not Mac-native*: Mac-idiom keyboard shortcuts (Cmd+arrow, Cmd+W, Cmd+, etc.), menu bar items where Mac idiom calls for them, window-resize handling consistent with macOS, and a polish pass on focus-ring / pointer-hover behaviors that the iPad codebase gets for free under iPadOS pointer support. Full macOS idiom (multi-window state restoration, document-based architecture, custom menu bar beyond iPad-app default) explicitly out of scope and would require superseding this ADR. Commitments 2–6 restate verbatim: cost-priced subscription via Apple In-App Purchase / no free tier (target $12.99/mo monthly with annual subscription option, Apple Small Business Program 15% take rate presumed, App Store refund window as the trial affordance); builder eats API costs within fixed annual operating subsidy budget / no grants / no 501(c)(3) / no institutional licensing; no BYOK / no institutional regime (OQ-BYOK-REGIME continues closed by foreclosure); [ADR 0029](adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md) cost ceiling reframed as fixed annual operating subsidy budget — nothing ever raises it; polish-static / maintenance-minimum-shape (no social, sharing, leaderboards, streaks, push notifications beyond auth/billing, community, in-app messaging — the "modest keyboard/menu polish" for Mac is consistent with the static-polish discipline). Success criterion: "an app I would pay for if it weren't mine" — restated verbatim from [ADR 0032](adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md). The reasoning chain that produced the broadening: the editorial / typographic / library-shaped product structure following from [ADR 0033](adr/0033-mission-realignment-structured-guidance-for-self-learners.md) / [ADR 0034](adr/0034-discovery-planning-engagement-triad.md) works best when larger screens (iPad, Mac via Designed-for-iPad) do the heavy work and the phone is a follow-up surface; serious philosophy reading benefits from iPad screen real estate; "Designed for iPad on Mac" is essentially free distribution (Apple Silicon Macs run iPad apps from the App Store by default unless the developer opts out). The disposition spirit survives the broadening intact: single-codebase / single-store / single-billing-path / single review queue / single privacy questionnaire / single refund window. The corruption-vector identification carried by [ADR 0032](adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md) ("leave the option open to expand later" was the seed pattern that pulled design toward business outcomes pedagogy never warranted) survives in this ADR and remains the discipline against which future supersessions are tested. Refusal-not-deferral commitment binding at the new boundary: Android, web, and native AppKit/Catalyst Mac each foreclosed; reopening any one of them requires superseding this ADR. Settles the Mac-via-Designed-for-iPad polish-depth question that [ADR 0034](adr/0034-discovery-planning-engagement-triad.md) flagged as downstream of S-0015 at "modest keyboard/menu polish." [ADR 0029](adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md)'s mechanism unchanged (multi-platform reach increases the surface where users discover the app, increasing the importance of the per-user cap doing its job; the broadening does not change what the cap is for). [ADR 0031](adr/0031-erasure-mechanism-and-individual-only-regime.md)'s erasure mechanism is platform-independent; hard-delete with cascade applies identically across all three Apple targets; Apple App Store guideline 5.1.1 (in-app account deletion) is satisfied for the iPad-app build that runs on Mac via Designed-for-iPad just as it is for the iPhone build. Does not rise to MISSION.md's strong-working-commitments list (operating discipline / platform scope, not pedagogical commitment — same precedent as ADRs 0026/0029/0031/0032/0033/0034). Status: Accepted.

- [`adr/0034-discovery-planning-engagement-triad.md`](adr/0034-discovery-planning-engagement-triad.md) — Discovery / Planning / Engagement triad as primary product structure. Replaces the globe-as-home-screen + concept-engagement-surface architecture retired by [ADR 0033](adr/0033-mission-realignment-structured-guidance-for-self-learners.md). Three primary surfaces, one each for the three structurally distinct problems the structured-guidance value claim answers: **Discovery** (figuring out what to learn at all — dual-path: AI conversational onboarding + browseable concept catalog; both committed first-class, neither a fallback for the other; both feed the same plan-generation pipeline downstream); **Planning** (knowing what to understand first — syllabus-as-plan, prerequisite gating, current/active syllabus view with the hard-cap-of-five preserved, quiet completion markers, mastered concepts visible in syllabus context, cross-syllabus convergence noting at the routing-after-concept-completion moment); **Engagement** (knowing whether you have actually learned the thing rather than become familiar with its facts — structurally inherited from [ADR 0028](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md): three bounded contexts — concept engagement Mode 2/3, diagnostic conversation, BYOB close reading per [ADR 0011](adr/0011-no-hosted-copyrighted-material.md); preserved unchanged). Cross-domain edges remain first-class graph data per [ADR 0007](adr/0007-cross-domain-porosity.md); UI rendering convention is **bridge surfacing in context** during planning (cross-syllabus convergence notes; plan-generation overlap flagging) and during engagement (callback references that bridge between domains; in-engagement surfacing of cross-domain prerequisites that have just become reachable). Explicit foreclosures: no globe; no game-world rendering; no separate trophy surface; no library/bookshelf as a third primary surface (mastered concepts surface contextually within syllabi, not as a standalone trophy); no mastery-glow / tendril / colored-trail visualization; no general chat surface (per [ADR 0028](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md)). Two open-for-amendment-without-supersession items flagged: library/bookshelf surface (if Phase 9 cold-test surfaces a concrete need for an aggregated mastered-concepts view consistent with the no-trophy-spectacle discipline) and discovery dual-path narrowing (if Phase 9 cold-test evidence makes the case for a single-path simplification). Discovery-side catalog organization may consume [ADR 0018](adr/0018-flat-domain-tags-community-detection.md)'s flat-domain-tags + community-detection algorithm as the concept-clustering primitive (the algorithm survives [ADR 0033](adr/0033-mission-realignment-structured-guidance-for-self-learners.md)'s globe drop because its consumer shifts; this ADR names the new consumer). Concurrent Syllabus Limit (hard cap of five) survives as a planning-surface constraint — the pedagogical rationale (insufficient momentum on more than five paths) survives; the visual-density-of-the-globe-itself signaling rationale dropped with the globe; the planning surface signals the cap directly when the user attempts to exceed it. Bidirectional with [ADR 0027](adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md)'s pending S-0016 forbidden-token revision: the surface around the agent does not invite game-master framing (no game-shaped surfaces in the triad), and the agent's voice does not reach for that framing (the rendering policy will rule it out). Does not rise to MISSION.md's strong-working-commitments list (product-structural, not pedagogical commitment — same precedent as ADRs 0026/0029/0031/0032/0033). Future feature design proposing a primary surface outside the triad must supersede this ADR; secondary surfaces (settings, account management, billing, delete-account, data-export, parked-syllabus list, user library of uploaded texts) do not require supersession. Status: Accepted.

### Changed (S-0014)
- [`docs/ui-architecture.md`](docs/ui-architecture.md) — substantial rewrite per ADR 0034. The prior **Globe Navigation Model** and **Level-of-Detail Rendering** sections (added 2026-04-07 / 2026-04-09) are dropped wholesale per [ADR 0033](adr/0033-mission-realignment-structured-guidance-for-self-learners.md). The file now describes the three primary surfaces (Discovery / Planning / Engagement) and their structural relationships: Discovery's dual-path affordances (AI conversational onboarding bounded by [ADR 0028](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md)'s purpose-not-topic discipline + browseable concept catalog whose organization may consume [ADR 0018](adr/0018-flat-domain-tags-community-detection.md)'s community-detection algorithm); Planning's affordances (syllabus-as-plan with prerequisite ordering and current position; prerequisite gating consuming the mastery model per [ADR 0009](adr/0009-portable-mastery.md) / [ADR 0023](adr/0023-engagement-depth-aggregation.md) / [ADR 0024](adr/0024-engagement-depth-sub-signals-stored-raw.md); quiet completion markers reflecting state, not generating reward feedback; current/active syllabus view with the hard-cap-of-five preserved and the planning surface signaling the cap directly when exceeded; cross-syllabus convergence noting at routing-after-concept-completion); Engagement's structural inheritance from [ADR 0028](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md) (three bounded contexts unchanged; exit affordance as first-class UI primitive returning to Planning or, for diagnostic exits, to Discovery). Cross-surface concerns documented: mastery state single-source-of-truth across surfaces, secondary surfaces enumerated (settings/account, delete-account, data-export, user library of uploaded texts, parked-syllabus list), surface-level foreclosures restated, render-readiness contract per [ADR 0027](adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md) applies across all surfaces. Bridge-surfacing-in-context as the cross-domain rendering convention (per [ADR 0007](adr/0007-cross-domain-porosity.md)) committed at two natural moments (planning's cross-syllabus convergence; engagement's callback references and in-engagement prerequisite surfacing).
- [`docs/session-lifecycle.md`](docs/session-lifecycle.md) — substantial rewrite per ADR 0034. The prior **Globe as Home Screen** section is dropped wholesale per [ADR 0033](adr/0033-mission-realignment-structured-guidance-for-self-learners.md); the trophy/glow/tendrils framing in **Mastery Verification Through Downstream Teaching** ("mastery glow activates and tendrils appear") is stripped and replaced with quiet-completion-marker framing on the Planning surface ("the syllabus marks the concept as mastered; cross-domain bridges surface contextually in subsequent engagement"). Preserved intact: **Concept Engagement as Atomic Unit** (the entire arc of working through one concept step on a syllabus, however many sittings it takes); **Concurrent Syllabus Limit** (hard cap of five; pedagogical rationale unchanged); **Mode Transitions** (1→2→3 teaching modes triggered by textual signals in the user's most recent response, with backward transitions when warranted); **Proficiency as Implied Transition** (quiet, never announced); **Routing After Concept Completion** (return to Planning surface; cross-syllabus convergence noting); **Mastery Verification Through Downstream Teaching** (organic-escalation framing per [ADR 0013](adr/0013-mastery-verification-organic-escalation.md) — callback references as pedagogical genuine + mastery probe + bridge-revealing where upstream concept lives in a neighboring domain; escalation to zero-scaffolding moment after sufficient distance; tonal shift as the only signal; quiet recognition tone after successful verification, intrinsic-not-extrinsic). New **Entry Surfaces** subsection at top documents how the user reaches concept engagement from the Planning surface; a new **Exit and Return** subsection at bottom documents the [ADR 0028](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md) exit affordance as first-class UI primitive returning to Planning (or Discovery for diagnostic exits) and the resumption-discipline preservation of atomic-unit framing across exit/return cycles.
- [`adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) — Phase 1.5 — Mission Realignment table extended with ADR 0034 (Status: Accepted); orientation paragraph updated to record S-0014 closure. ADR count after S-0014: 34 ADRs total — 33 Accepted plus 1 Superseded.
- MemPalace decision drawer for ADR 0034 filed (verbatim conversational reasoning per the two-layer decision-recording discipline in CLAUDE.md). Drawer carries: the gap [ADR 0033](adr/0033-mission-realignment-structured-guidance-for-self-learners.md) left (closure without replacement); the structural decomposition of the value claim (three problems → three surfaces, one-to-one); the discovery-side dual-path commitment rationale (autodidact-with-target deserves catalog without conversation; freshman-without-target deserves conversation without catalog navigation; forcing one path is a category error against [ADR 0012](adr/0012-freshman-defaults-autodidact-ceiling.md)); the library/bookshelf foreclosure rationale (re-introduces the corruption vector under a new name); cross-domain bridge-surfacing-in-context as the durable convention; the open-for-amendment-without-supersession items (library/bookshelf, discovery dual-path) and why they are not as foundational as the no-globe decision.

### Added (S-0013 — Phase 1.5 opens: mission realignment as structured guidance for self-learners)
- [`adr/0033-mission-realignment-structured-guidance-for-self-learners.md`](adr/0033-mission-realignment-structured-guidance-for-self-learners.md) — Mission realignment: structured guidance for self-learners. Records the corruption vector identified across the multi-turn S-0008–S-0013 exploration arc: the globe / mastery-glow / cross-domain-tendrils / trophy / "knowledge as a world" UI metaphor was a UI-layer optimization that drifted attention away from the project's core value claim — *filling the gap a self-learner has when there is no teacher to open doors and show the way.* The diagnosis: form (spatial-traversal UI with character-on-map framing, mastery glow, trophy framing) signals casual play / low stakes; content (phenomenology, advanced epistemology, cross-domain bridges) demands contemplation / sustained attention / real difficulty; cold-test users absorb form before content; a casual-register form makes the contemplation-register content fight uphill on every concept engagement. Compounds with [ADR 0032](adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md) commitment 6's foreclosure of social/sharing/leaderboards/streaks — the globe + reward visualization pulls toward the gamification ADR 0032 forecloses, even when those mechanics are absent in code (users' game-shaped expectations don't read source, they read the surface). Records the deliberate architectural removal (not deferral) of: globe-as-home-screen, mastery glow as visual feedback, cross-domain tendrils as visual representation, trophy framing of the globe, "exploring a world / territory of knowledge" framing, "knowledge as a world" metaphor. Names what survives intact: pedagogical dependency graph as data ([ADR 0001](adr/0001-pedagogical-edges-not-historical.md), [ADR 0017](adr/0017-postgres-recursive-ctes-over-owl-rdf.md), [ADR 0030](adr/0030-confidence-level-evidentiary-mode-on-nodes.md)); concept-not-thinker granularity ([ADR 0008](adr/0008-concept-nodes-not-thinkers.md)); cross-domain porosity as data ([ADR 0007](adr/0007-cross-domain-porosity.md)) — bridges remain first-class graph elements with UI rendering becoming contextual surfacing during engagement and planning per ADR 0034 at S-0014; mastery model ([ADR 0009](adr/0009-portable-mastery.md), [ADR 0010](adr/0010-continuous-contextual-assessment.md), [ADR 0013](adr/0013-mastery-verification-organic-escalation.md), [ADR 0023](adr/0023-engagement-depth-aggregation.md), [ADR 0024](adr/0024-engagement-depth-sub-signals-stored-raw.md), [ADR 0025](adr/0025-historical-maximum-tracking.md)); AI instructor split ([ADR 0014](adr/0014-sonnet-teaches-opus-reviews.md)); bring-your-own-book close reading ([ADR 0011](adr/0011-no-hosted-copyrighted-material.md), [ADR 0005](adr/0005-per-text-interpretive-outline.md)); privacy posture ([ADR 0026](adr/0026-persistent-learner-storage-structural-not-substantive.md), [ADR 0031](adr/0031-erasure-mechanism-and-individual-only-regime.md)); cost ceiling ([ADR 0029](adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md)); bounded engagement contexts ([ADR 0028](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md)); personal-project disposition commitments 2–6 from [ADR 0032](adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md) (commitment 1 broadens at S-0015 in ADR 0035 to iPhone + iPad + Mac via Designed-for-iPad). Names the mission as **structured guidance for self-learners**: graph answers *what to learn and in what order*; instructor answers *did you actually learn it*. Names the cascade of paired artifacts: ADR 0034 (replacement structure — Discovery / Planning / Engagement triad) at S-0014; ADR 0035 (platform-scope supersession) at S-0015; revision to [ADR 0027](adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md) (forbidden-token additions for globe / reward / territory / exploration language) at S-0016. Closure is structural in the success case per the [ADR 0032](adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md) refusal-not-deferral pattern — future "could we add a globe" proposals must supersede this ADR; per-session re-litigation not authorized. Does not rise to MISSION.md's strong-working-commitments list (operating discipline precedent — same as ADRs 0026/0029/0031/0032). Records corruption-vector test for future sessions: does this proposal commit to a presentation surface before the value claim it serves is sharp? If yes, sharpen the value claim first. Records recovery from a silent drop (the Phase 1.5 plan approved via plan-mode at S-0013 boot landed at `/Users/shanekidd/.claude/plans/at-its-core-this-iterative-beaver.md` — local developer config, not tracked project artifacts; the recovery — recording Phase 1.5 in ROADMAP.md / STATE.md / ADR 0033 — is part of S-0013's scope; lesson: plan-mode artifacts do not propagate into the project's session protocol on their own). Status: Accepted.
- [`ROADMAP.md`](ROADMAP.md) — new **Phase 1.5 (Mission Realignment Overhaul)** section inserted between Phase 1 (closed at S-0012) and Phase 2 (Build Plan Scaffolding, queued for S-0017). Phase 1.5 sits between the closed Phase 1 and the queued Phase 2 because Phase 2 will scaffold per-session contracts for every downstream phase, and those scaffolds would lock in the wrong UI architecture and platform scope if Phase 2 ran before the realignment lands. Phase 1.5 spans four sessions and is **realignment, not rebuild** — the pedagogical dependency graph, AI instructor model, BYOB close reading, mastery model, privacy posture, and cost ceiling all survive intact. Sub-phases named: 1.5.1 (S-0013, this session) — ADR 0033 mission realignment + globe/reward closure; light revisions to ADR 0018 and MISSION.md What this is. 1.5.2 (S-0014) — ADR 0034 Discovery / Planning / Engagement triad; substantial rewrites of `docs/ui-architecture.md` and `docs/session-lifecycle.md`. 1.5.3 (S-0015) — ADR 0035 multi-platform Apple expansion (supersedes ADR 0032); ROADMAP Phase 9 rewrite; business.md Pricing and Distribution amendment. 1.5.4 (S-0016) — ADR 0027 forbidden-token extension; AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md update; light revisions to ADRs 0012 and 0014; sweep across ~10 secondary docs. Phase 1.5 success criteria: ADRs 0033/0034/0035 land Accepted, ADR 0032 superseded, foundational doc rewrites complete, zero residual globe/glow/tendril references in tracked artifacts (modulo deliberate historical references in CHANGELOG and the recording ADRs themselves), Phase 9 success criteria rewritten, Phase 2 opens at S-0017 with the realigned contract as input. Plan reference noted: `/Users/shanekidd/.claude/plans/at-its-core-this-iterative-beaver.md` (approved at S-0013 boot, local developer config not a tracked artifact).

### Added (S-0012 — Phase 1 fully closes: project-direction supersession; ADR 0002 retired)
- [`adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md`](adr/0032-personal-project-disposition.md) — Personal project disposition; refusal-not-deferral commercial closure. **Supersedes [ADR 0002](adr/0002-commercial-sustainability-without-pedagogical-compromise.md).** Six binding commitments record the project disposition settled in the S-0011 conversation: (1) single-platform iOS via App Store; (2) cost-priced subscription via Apple In-App Purchase, no free tier (target $12.99/mo monthly with annual subscription option, Apple Small Business Program 15% take rate presumed, App Store refund window as the trial affordance); (3) builder eats API costs within a fixed annual operating subsidy budget, no grants, no 501(c)(3), no institutional licensing; (4) no bring-your-own-key, neither consumer nor institutional, no institutional regime (OQ-BYOK-REGIME closes by foreclosure); (5) [ADR 0029](adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md) cost ceiling reframed as fixed annual operating subsidy budget — nothing ever raises it (mechanism unchanged; justification structure changed); (6) polish is static, never dynamic, maintenance is minimum-shape (no social, sharing, leaderboards, streaks, push notifications beyond auth/billing, community, in-app messaging). Success criterion: "an app I would pay for if it weren't mine" — self-applying, defended against builder-bias drift by [ADR 0012](adr/0012-freshman-defaults-autodidact-ceiling.md) and [ADR 0027](adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md) (now load-bearing for builder-bias protection in addition to their original load-bearing roles). Refusal-not-deferral commitment binding in the success case: *"if this scales beyond what the personal subsidy budget supports, the response is to raise prices to slow growth or to cap signups, not to pursue institutional clients, grants, or acquisition."* Corruption-vector identification: "leave the option open to expand later" was the seed pattern that pulled the design toward business outcomes pedagogy never warranted; the fix is removing the optionality, not strengthening the guard ([ADR 0002](adr/0002-commercial-sustainability-without-pedagogical-compromise.md)) against the mechanisms the optionality preserved. Does not rise to MISSION.md's strong-working-commitments list (operating discipline, not pedagogical commitment) — same precedent as ADRs 0026 / 0029 / 0031. Status: Accepted.

### Added (S-0011 — Phase 1 close: privacy ADRs collapsed under project-direction shift)
- [`adr/0031-erasure-mechanism-and-individual-only-regime.md`](adr/0031-erasure-mechanism-and-individual-only-regime.md) — Erasure mechanism (hard-delete with cascade); individual-only data regime. Settles **OQ-PRIVACY-A** as hard-delete-with-cascade — `ON DELETE CASCADE` foreign-key discipline across `learner_events`, `mastery_snapshots`, and `tension_log` carries deletion through to all rows linked to a user; Apple App Store guideline 5.1.1 (in-app account deletion) is satisfied at the schema level. Withdraws **OQ-PRIVACY-B** as moot — the project no longer pursues an institutional regime; `cohort_id` is removed from [ADR 0026](adr/0026-persistent-learner-storage-structural-not-substantive.md) sub-decision (2)'s `learner_events.context` shape (surviving columns: `path_id`, `source_text_id`, `session_id`); the institutional schema provisions in `docs/architecture.md` become dead-weight whose removal lands in S-0012. Two rejected candidates from OQ-PRIVACY-A recorded as rejected: **crypto-shredding** (per-learner KMS keys earn their keep only when audit-trail-preserving erasure is contractually required — a posture the project no longer pursues) and **anonymize-and-aggregate** (graph-level signal contribution from a single user's events is negligible at consumer scale, and event sparsity makes residual data potentially re-identifiable). The simplification was enabled by the project-direction shift settled in S-0011 conversation: single-platform iOS App Store consumer subscription, no institutional regime, no BYOK, no enterprise wrapper, no grants, no 501(c)(3), no acquisition exit. The supersession ADR formalizing that shift (retiring [ADR 0002](adr/0002-commercial-sustainability-without-pedagogical-compromise.md)) is queued for S-0012. The dependency is named explicitly in ADR 0031's Consequences; if S-0012 surfaces a complication, ADR 0031 may require revision (low-risk because the commitment was settled in user-directing form within S-0011's exploration). Status: Accepted.

### Added (S-0010 — Phase 1.3: `confidence_level` column on Node Schema; closes Phase 1 modulo OQ-PRIVACY-A/B)
- [`adr/0030-confidence-level-evidentiary-mode-on-nodes.md`](adr/0030-confidence-level-evidentiary-mode-on-nodes.md) — `confidence_level` is the evidentiary-mode axis on nodes. Establishes the column as a third epistemic axis orthogonal to `provenance` (who authored, lifecycle stage) and to numeric `confidence` (how-sure-now, updates with evidence). The column records *what kind of evidence backed the node's existence at authoring time* and is fixed-at-write — supersession (per [ADR 0021](adr/0021-node-deprecation-status-superseded-by.md)) is the channel for changing it, not in-place update. Enum semantics: **EXTRACTED** (lifted from a source's own structuring — SEP TOC, curriculum prerequisite list, graph dataset; vocabulary alignment not concept invention), **INTERPRETED** (pedagogical inference from source material that does not itself structure around the concept; Phase 5.2 baseline per "mark INTERPRETED until validated"), **SYNTHETIC** (generated wholesale; service nodes terminating cross-domain prerequisite chains, Opus-batch-proposed splits without source basis; first candidates for self-correction review). Default `'INTERPRETED'` matches Phase 5.2 baseline; EXTRACTED would silently overclaim source backing on forgot-the-column writes; SYNTHETIC would over-flag the Phase 4 review queue. Two orthogonality test combinations recorded inline (`provenance='human'` + `confidence_level='SYNTHETIC'` for human-authored service nodes; `confidence=0.3` + `confidence_level='EXTRACTED'` for source-aligned nodes whose belief decayed under counter-evidence — the label does not update with that decay; the numeric belief does). Naming risk acknowledged: `confidence_level` reads as a finer version of `confidence` despite being a categorical evidentiary mode rather than a numeric belief — the name is settled across STATE.md / ROADMAP.md / ADR 0016 / Phase 5.2; renaming would invalidate downstream references; the ADR's Decision section is the durable mitigation. Storage representation: `TEXT` not Postgres ENUM, following `provenance` and `status` precedent — adding a new value is a superseding ADR + Phase 4 audit update, not a migration. Status: Accepted.

Column justification expanded inline with the three enum values, their semantics (with the Phase 5.2 INTERPRETED baseline and the SYNTHETIC review-queue cross-link), the orthogonality argument (categorical evidentiary mode vs. numeric belief vs. authoring channel), and the fixed-at-write update discipline. The existing `confidence` column entry now explicitly notes it "updates over time" to distinguish from the new column. ### Added (S-0008 — Phase 1.2: rendering policy + sibling commitments from exploration)
- [`AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md`](AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md) — the rendering-policy contract; ships verbatim as Sonnet's system prompt at Phase 7. Eight sections (role; expression contract — three teaching modes; voice and prose discipline; forbidden tokens with per-category ADR-pointer rationale; surviving tokens; citation rules; uncertainty posture; scope discipline per ADR 0028; tension emission per ADR 0026; worked example with stub input + pass-case output annotated; pre-send self-check). The forbidden-token enumeration is the load-bearing surface — additions are CHANGELOG-tracked, removals require a superseding ADR. The worked example is the gradeable test artifact for Phase 7 success criterion (zero forbidden-token leakage on 10 random concept queries).
- [`adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md`](adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md) — Rendering policy as the prompt-layer contract for the teaching agent. Establishes [`AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md`](AGENT_INSTRUCTIONS.md) as the shipping artifact, the asymmetric-amendment discipline (additions cheap, removals require ADR), the Phase 7 graded test, the Phase 4 `tools/validate.py` rendering-audit category, and the structurally-enforced-vs-aspirational shift for the [ADR 0012](adr/0012-freshman-defaults-autodidact-ceiling.md) audience commitment. Pairs with [ADR 0028](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md) as input-output contract. Status: Accepted.
- [`adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md`](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md) — Input-side scope is structural, not prompt-policed. Three reasons prompt-level guardrails fail (leaky-in-both-directions, over-rejects Mode 3, gradual-drift equilibrium); three bounded input contexts (concept engagement, diagnostic, bring-your-own-book close reading); within-context discrimination is purpose-not-topic by speech-act (bringing material vs. redirecting tasks); exit affordance UI primitive as the structural alternative to general chat; prompt-level off-topic-refusal language explicitly forbidden (would over-reject the cross-context Mode 3 connections the design depends on). The "architectural-constraint-beats-prompt-guardrail" principle is recorded as a citable commitment generalizing beyond input scope. Pairs with [ADR 0027](adr/0027-rendering-policy-prompt-layer-contract.md). Status: Accepted.
- [`adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md`](adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md) — Personal financial cost ceiling is an operating constraint. Three architectural commitments: (1) cost protection is a precondition (not a feature) for opening to non-builder users — no phase opens that surface without a cost-cap mechanism wired and tested (per-user cap, aggregate cap, real-time telemetry, defined cap-behavior); (2) architectural choices evaluated against this constraint — institutional BYOK and seasonal pre-buy raised in priority; "ask Paideia anything" general chat foreclosed by combination with [ADR 0028](adr/0028-input-side-scope-structural-not-prompt.md); (3) cap-behavior must preserve concept-engagement integrity — soft walls *degrade* (Opus → Sonnet → shallower retrieval) rather than terminate mid-engagement. The numeric ceiling is private operational configuration, not a public artifact. Does not rise to MISSION.md commitments list (operating discipline, not pedagogical commitment) — same precedent as [ADR 0026](adr/0026-persistent-learner-storage-structural-not-substantive.md). Status: Accepted.
- [`docs/pedagogy/inferences.md`](docs/pedagogy/inferences.md) — Pedagogical Inference Registry stub. Seed inventory of ~19 inferences across mode classification, mastery state, mastery verification, path/traversal, tension emission, and concept-engagement-lifecycle categories, each with trigger / action / lives-in (design) / lives-in (code) / notes. Plus an "open inferences" section naming five inferences the design implies but has not yet specified. Created per OQ-PEDAGOGY-INFERENCE-LOCUS in [`docs/tensions.md`](docs/tensions.md) as the cheap intermediate step before deciding whether to build a dedicated rule layer. Maintenance discipline: add a row when a new inference is committed; revisit the rule-layer question when the registry crosses ~30 entries.
- [`docs/tensions.md`](docs/tensions.md) — Four open questions added per S-0008's exploration commitments:
  - **OQ-BYOK-REGIME** (institutional vs. consumer bring-your-own-key) — institutional BYOK keep open as primary non-builder access path; consumer BYOK foreclose unless future regime change justifies revisiting. Decide-before any non-builder consumer launch (Phase 8 entry or earlier). Per [ADR 0029](adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md).
  - **OQ-WALL-BEHAVIOR** (soft-wall degradation ladder at cost cap) — five candidate steps (model downshift, retrieval shrink, cross-domain bridge cap, concept-engagement length cap, soft refusal). Open: order, trigger thresholds, per-user vs. per-aggregate, user notification. Decide-before Phase 8 cost-cap mechanism wiring. Per [ADR 0029](adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md).
  - **OQ-CONTEXT-COMPRESSION** (token-amplification mitigation for multi-turn concept engagements) — three candidates: (a) structured-state replacement, (b) automatic context compression at platform-supported windows, (c) explicit per-turn summarization. Leaning shape: (a) + (c) with (b) as transparent layer; not yet settled because parameters and cost-quality tradeoffs not measured. Decide-before Phase 7 (Sonnet teaching prototype). Per [ADR 0029](adr/0029-personal-financial-cost-ceiling.md).
  - **OQ-PEDAGOGY-INFERENCE-LOCUS** (rule layer vs. distributed inference; tagged `watch`) — standing position is distributed code is appropriate; the registry [`docs/pedagogy/inferences.md`](docs/pedagogy/inferences.md) created as forcing function for the population to become visible. Two failure modes a rule layer would risk (conflict accumulation, performance opacity); one thing it would buy (declarative review by non-engineers). Revisit when registry crosses ~30 entries OR cross-domain edges per domain-pair exceed ~50 OR an operational complaint surfaces.
